<p>The Light stat was a special attribute, so the chances of it dropping weren’t high. Zhou Wen had never downloaded a Light-elemental zone, so he hadn’t had many Light-elemental crystals drop. He was far from reaching the Light stat requirements.</p>
<p>Just as Zhou Wen was feeling depressed, he suddenly realized that one of the dimensional crystals that Starlord Ravenous Wolf dropped was Light-elemental.</p>
<p>1</p>
<p>Without any hesitation, he absorbed the Light stat crystal that nearly reached 300 in value.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen achieved 99 Light stat points. This was the limit at the Terror grade as he hadn’t advanced to the Calamity grade. No matter how high the stat crystals he absorbed were, it was impossible for him to continue raising his stats.</p>
<p>This really doesn’t make sense. The limit of the Mythical stage’s stats is 81, but the limit of the Terror grade’s stats is 99. Isn’t the difference too small? Zhou Wen found it odd. The difference in values between the other levels was huge. It was about double. Only the difference between the Mythical stage and the Terror grade was tiny. He didn’t know why.</p>
<p>That was what he thought, but he could only come to terms with the reality. No matter how unreasonable it was, it couldn’t be changed. He could only adapt.</p>
<p>Thankfully, with 99 points of Light stats, he satisfied the requirements needed to absorb the skill crystal. What was lacking now was a Light-stat Terror transformation ability.</p>
<p>Among the Essence Energy Arts I simulated, the only one that can be associated with light is the Ancient Sovereign Sutra. That flame of life should be considered light, right? Zhou Wen wasn’t sure as he switched his Essence Energy Art to the Ancient Sovereign Sutra. Then, he picked up the skill crystal and attempted to absorb it.</p>
<p>Immediately, a hot and numbing force flowed out of the skill crystal and rushed into Zhou Wen’s body, making his entire body feel like it was being baked by high temperatures.</p>
<p>Thankfully, he was in-game. If he were outside, Zhou Wen’s clothes would have been burned to ashes by the high temperature.</p>
<p>The terrifying energy barbarically opened up a new Essence Energy circulation in Zhou Wen’s body. The terrifyingly high temperature and radiation energy made Zhou Wen believe that the blood-colored avatar’s body was about to collapse.</p>
<p>Thankfully, he ultimately survived and absorbed Starlord Ravenous Wolf’s skill crystal.</p>
<p>‘Absorbed Starlord Ravenous Wolf Crystal. Attained Hell-level Essence Energy Skill: Wolf Kiss.’</p>
<p>Wolf Kiss! Zhou Wen sensed the skill information from the Essence Energy Crystal and his expression turned odd. He opened the skill column and saw that it was indeed Wolf Kiss.</p>
<p>Wolf Kiss (Hell): The Ravenous Wolf Star is the Star of Desire. The Ravenous Wolf’s Kiss is earth-shattering.</p>
<p>What the hell! Zhou Wen was at a loss whether to laugh or cry. He originally imagined that with Starlord Ravenous Wolf’s powerful abilities, any random skill like a light blast, radiation, or high temperature would greatly increase the destructive power of his skills. To his surprise, he ended up with Wolf Kiss.</p>
<p>The skill introduction sounded very strong, but Zhou Wen couldn’t be hugging the enemy and kissing them amid his battle, right?</p>
<p>Zhou Wen imagined a scene of him fighting An Tianzuo. At the brink of losing, he could only use the only Hell-level skill he had—Wolf Kiss—to turn the tables.</p>
<p>1</p>
<p>He then took the opportunity to hug An Tianzuo’s head and use Wolf Kiss. It was an unbearable sight.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen definitely hadn’t misunderstood the language describing the skill’s usage because the information had been transmitted to his brain by the Essence Energy Crystal. That was exactly how Wolf Kiss was used.</p>
<p>How can I use this skill! Zhou Wen was so depressed that he nearly vomited blood.</p>
<p>This skill wasn’t suitable to be used against men. If it was used on monsters, even if Zhou Wen could bring himself to kiss them, many monsters’ mouths would be extremely large. Ignoring kissing, Zhou Wen would just be giving them more protein if he really leaned his head over.</p>
<p>1</p>
<p>Although he didn’t know how powerful Wolf Kiss was, Zhou Wen was certain that he couldn’t use it casually.</p>
<p>Just like kowtowing could trigger the Sigh of the King—something Zhou Wen knew was useful—but he really couldn’t bring himself into such embarrassment. Most of the time, Zhou Wen was embarrassed to use that move.</p>
<p>Wolf Kiss was about the same, but Zhou Wen realized that he could use it at times after some thought.</p>
<p>He distributed the other stat crystals to the Companion Beasts that needed them. Banana Fairy’s stats were already maxed out. It was useless eating them without leveling up. The Soul Mirror was almost maxed as well. Raising stats wasn’t difficult for Zhou Wen. The difficult part was how to raise the level.</p>
<p>“If Banana Fairy can advance to the Calamity grade, she might be able to extinguish the sun with a gust of Supreme Yin Wind. I wouldn’t need to go through so much trouble!”</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was just musing. If he wanted to extinguish the sun, it was unknown if the Apocalypse grade could do it, much less the Calamity grade.</p>
<p>After tidying up everything, Zhou Wen circled the palace again and realized that there was only one hall. There were no other exits behind it, nor were there any other palaces.</p>
<p>At the back of the palace was a strange altar. On it seemed to be some kind of runes used for rituals.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen controlled the blood-colored avatar to stand on it as a notification popped up in-game: Do you want to teleport to Merak Star Palace?</p>
<p>Zhou Wen immediately understood that the Big Dipper instance dungeon was indeed a serial dungeon. He guessed that there was a dungeon on each of the Big Dipper stars. He had to clear all seven dungeons to clear the Big Dipper instance dungeon.</p>
<p>Starlord Ravenous Wolf in the first dungeon is at the Hell level. Typically, dungeons become stronger the further one goes. I wonder how strong the dimensional creatures in the next six dungeons will be. Zhou Wen thought for a moment and chose no.</p>
<p>He wanted to see what would happen if he chose no.</p>
<p>System Notice: Do you want to teleport out of Dubhe Palace?</p>
<p>Zhou Wen immediately chose ‘yes’ to see where he would teleport to.</p>
<p>The teleportation nexus flashed as the scene in front of Zhou Wen changed. There were dazzling flames everywhere. Zhou Wen looked around and realized that he was at the periphery of Dubhe.</p>
<p>There’s a way to return! Zhou Wen was overjoyed.</p>
<h3 id='chapter1542'>Chapter 1542: Starlord Titan Gate</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>
<p>Since the seven dungeons of the Big Dipper were separated, Zhou Wen could freely choose to continue heading to the next Star Palace after completing Dubhe. That was his chance.</p>
<p>All he needed to do was use the Cube to enter Dubhe Palace and clear it in reality. Then, he could teleport out and return to Earth.</p>
<p>From the looks of it, this was the only way to return to Earth before Demonic Neonate woke up.</p>
<p>It was no longer difficult for Zhou Wen to clear Dubhe Palace and kill Starlord Ravenous Wolf.</p>
<p>The more troublesome thing was Demonic Neonate and Grim Demon. Furthermore, he needed to find three people to ascend the Cube with him before he could activate the Cube and enter Dubhe Palace.</p>
<p>Demonic Neonate was still sleeping and showed no signs of waking up. Furthermore, he couldn’t unsummon her. He couldn’t even send her into the chaos space.</p>
<p>It wasn’t impossible for him to carry her into Dubhe Palace, but Zhou Wen didn’t wish for so many people to see Demonic Neonate through the broadcast.</p>
<p>The most troublesome thing was to find three people to enter Dubhe Palace with him. The three would definitely die.</p>
<p>Although there were many people in Regretless City and it wasn’t difficult to find three people to send themselves to their deaths, Zhou Wen wasn’t such a person. He really couldn’t bring himself into forcing people with whom he had no grudge to die.</p>
<p>I’ll wait another two days before reassessing. It’s best if Demonic Neonate wakes up. If she doesn’t, I can only use the Cube to return. Zhou Wen launched the Big Dipper instance dungeon again.</p>
<p>After entering Dubhe Palace again, there was no Starlord Ravenous Wolf guarding it. From the looks of it, it hadn’t respawned.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen arrived at the teleportation nexus and chose to enter the next Merak Star Palace.</p>
<p>Merak was the second star of the Big Dipper. Merak was also known as the Titan Gate Star. According to what Zhou Wen knew, although Merak was several times bigger than the sun, there didn’t seem to be any planets around Merak. There was only a ring of relatively cold dust.</p>
<p>When the teleportation nexus was activated, the scene in front of Zhou Wen changed. When he regained his vision, he realized that a huge door had appeared in front of him. The door looked like the Arc de Triomphe, but it was even more majestic. It was probably a thousand meters tall and was carved from golden crystal. Standing in front of the extremely majestic door, Zhou Wen found himself as tiny as an ant.</p>
<p>And this was only the entrance to the Merak Star Palace. It was unimaginable how big the entire Star Palace was.</p>
<p>The Merak Star Palace had an entrance without a door. Zhou Wen stood on the steps outside the entrance and could see the scene inside.</p>
<p>The interior of the Star Palace was equally huge. It was more than enough to fly a helicopter inside. There were resplendent crystal pillars and walls everywhere.</p>
<p>Unlike Dubhe Palace’s simplicity, this Star Palace was extremely beautiful. The various carvings were opulent.</p>
<p>And at the back of the Star Palace, there was a huge crystal throne. A giant wearing golden crystal armor was sitting on the crystal throne with one hand supporting his chin as though he was deep in thought.</p>
<p>What a tall giant. Just sitting there makes it look about two hundred meters tall! Zhou Wen guessed what dimensional creature it was from the its appearance.</p>
<p>Since the guardian of Dubhe was Starlord Ravenous Wolf, this person was undoubtedly Starlord Titan Gate.</p>
<p>Just as Zhou Wen was pondering over it, Starlord Titan Gate opened his eyes. The eyes that were much bigger than car wheels opened as they emitted a terrifying golden glow. He stared at the spot where the blood-colored avatar was standing and slowly stood up.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen had never seen a dimensional creature’s aura as terrifying as Starlord Titan Gate’s. Perhaps other creatures were stronger than him, but in terms of aura, they might not be able to suppress him.</p>
<p>Looking at Starlord Titan Gate, Zhou Wen couldn’t help but think of the word “indomitable.”</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was already prepared to fight a tough battle. From the size of Starlord Titan Gate, he knew that his body was definitely extremely powerful with extremely violent strength.</p>
<p>The Chaos Egg could withstand the blast of light because it was an area-of-effect attack, resulting in greatly scattered strength. Zhou Wen wasn’t sure if the Chaos Egg could withstand a Strength-type dimensional creature like Starlord Titan Gate.</p>
<p>If I really can’t block his attacks, I can only place my hopes on dodging. Unfortunately, I gave my Heavenly Robe and lucky equipment to Wang Lu. Otherwise, it shouldn’t be difficult for me to dodge Starlord Titan Gate’s attack… Zhou Wen was still thinking of a countermeasure when he suddenly saw Starlord Titan Gate open his mouth.</p>
<p>In the next moment, a terrifying roar burst out of Starlord Titan Gate’s mouth, forming a sonic boom that instantly struck Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen never expected such a move. He imagined that Starlord Titan Gate was a Strength-type, so he never expected him to have a sonar attack.</p>
<p>Thankfully, Zhou Wen had fast reflexes. He summoned the Chaos Egg and protected himself.</p>
<p>When the sonic boom struck the Chaos Egg, a large number of solid Essence Energy Crystals were immediately produced inside. The number was about the same as when Starlord Ravenous Wolf attacked.</p>
<p>From the looks of it, Starlord Titan Gate should also be at the Hell level. That’s good. Zhou Wen felt relieved.</p>
<p>If the Star Palaces were each stronger than the last in the Big Dipper instance dungeons, it was unimaginable how strong the guardian inside the final Star Palace would be. It would be impossible to clear it.</p>
<p>Starlord Titan Gate wasn’t much stronger than Starlord Ravenous Wolf. This gave Zhou Wen hope. Perhaps the seven Starlords of the Big Dipper were all at the Hell level, so he still had a chance of clearing the Big Dipper.</p>
<p>Although similar in strength to Starlord Ravenous Wolf, Starlord Titan Gate’s abilities were completely different. His sonic attack and Starlord Ravenous Wolf’s sonic booms were from completely different systems.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen relied on the Chaos Egg to take a beating. At the same time, he summoned the Golden Wyrm Scissors and ordered it to attack Starlord Titan Gate.</p>
<p>However, not long after the Golden Wyrm Scissors flew out, its flying speed became slower and slower. Before it reached Starlord Titan Gate, the Golden Wyrm Scissors stopped.</p>
<p>No way? Starlord Titan Gate’s howl is so powerful that even the Golden Wyrm Scissors’ attack can’t completely tear through it? Zhou Wen was alarmed.</p>
<p>Something even more unbelievable happened next. The Golden Wyrm Scissors flew back and fiercely rushed at the Chaos Egg.</p>
<p>The Chaos Egg had no chance of dodging amidst the sonic booms. As for the Golden Wyrm Scissors’ destructive power, even the Chaos Egg couldn’t completely withstand it. A hole was torn open at the snipping point.</p>
<p>The howl rushed in through the hole, and then the phone screen went black.</p>
<p>What happened? Why did the Golden Wyrm Scissors suddenly turn against me? Zhou Wen hurriedly checked the Golden Wyrm Scissors’ information and realized that it was still intact. It was still his Companion Beast, so there wasn’t any problem.</p>
<p>However, he couldn’t figure out why the Golden Wyrm Scissors had suddenly lost control and attacked him.</p>
<h3 id='chapter1543'>Chapter 1543: Jiuyang</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>
<p>Starlord Titan Gate’s body doesn’t appear to be Strength-type, but sound-type. That’s quite surprising, Zhou Wen thought to himself. Furthermore, it should be Epsilon Ursae Majoris that represents sound, so why is Starlord Titan Gate a sound-type dimensional creature?</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was momentarily at a loss. However, he was certain that the sonar shockwave alone wasn’t enough to make the Golden Wyrm Scissors attack its owner. There had to be other forces behind this.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen entered the dungeon a few more times and quickly figured out what was going on.</p>
<p>Starlord Titan Gate’s roar was indeed a sound-type ability. Furthermore, this sound-type power wasn’t just a vibrational attack. It also had powers similar to bewitchment.</p>
<p>That power was useless against Zhou Wen who was wearing the Truth Listener earring, but the Golden Wyrm Scissors and other Companion Beasts couldn’t seem to withstand the assault of that power. As long as they were too far from Zhou Wen, they could easily betray him.</p>
<p>This left Zhou Wen depressed. His strength wasn’t enough to fight Starlord Titan Gate. Now, he was relying on his Companion Beasts to keep him going. It was a serious problem if his Companion Beasts betrayed him if they were too far from him.</p>
<p>From the looks of it, I’ll have to grind a few more times to study Starlord Titan Gate’s other weaknesses. Zhou Wen repeatedly grinded the Merak Star Palace. Although he was killed by Starlord Titan Gate every time, he still enjoyed it.</p>
<p>While Zhou Wen was studying Starlord Titan Gate, the various factions on Earth were still working hard on how to enter Dubhe Palace alive. All the fire-elemental dimensional creatures were repeatedly slaughtered by the various factions, pushing the prices of high-level fire-elemental defensive Companion Beasts to ridiculous levels.</p>
<p>Just as the various factions were gathering fire-elemental armor, the Cube’s screen stirred again. Someone had entered Dubhe Palace, and it was a human.</p>
<p>It was a young man in gorgeous armor who looked to be in his twenties or thirties.</p>
<p>“Human? How did he enter? How did he withstand such high temperatures?” No one knew the young man as they whispered.</p>
<p>“That’s strange. Isn’t it said that only four people can enter? Why is he alone?”</p>
<p>“What’s the point of entering? Under that blast of light, even the extremely powerful dinosaurs can’t withstand it. Death simply awaits him. From the looks of it, it should be a suicide squad from some faction used to scout the way, right?”</p>
<p>“There’s no doubt about it.”</p>
<p>“What a pity. He’s so handsome, but he’s dying just like that.” Women tended to focus on different things from men.</p>
<p>“Damn! I wonder which family’s the one letting such a young man die.”</p>
<p>The handsome young man couldn’t hear the discussions. Even if he heard them, he couldn’t be bothered.</p>
<p>He walked towards the Star Palace’s door one step after another, extended his flawless hands that were even more beautiful than a woman’s, and pushed open Dubhe Palace’s door.</p>
<p>Looking at Starlord Ravenous Wolf in the Star Palace, the young man walked in without any hesitation. When Starlord Ravenous Wolf saw someone enter the Star Palace, he unleashed a terrifying blast of light without a word.</p>
<p>The entire Star Palace and the square outside were instantly enveloped by the purple light blast. There were no blind spots.</p>
<p>The live broadcast of the Cube had been processed by the Cube. Even an ordinary person could see the young man’s figure in the blast of light.</p>
<p>Everyone thought that he was doomed, but in the blast of light, the young man didn’t show the horror and shock they had imagined.</p>
<p>The blast of light didn’t reduce his body to ashes. It didn’t even damage his hair. The armor on the young man’s body emitted a blinding light that was even more dazzling than the light blast. It was as though he was augmented by the sun.</p>
<p>“How… How is this possible… He’s actually fine… under such high temperatures and radiation… Is he still human?”</p>
<p>“When did such a young powerhouse appear among us humans?”</p>
<p>“Could he be Human Sovereign?”</p>
<p>Ordinary people discussed spiritedly as they guessed the young man’s origins. As for factions like the six families, they had already identified the young man’s background.</p>
<p>“Solar Holy Body. That young man should be from the Holy Land’s Sun God Holy Temple. I never expected the Holy Land to take action so quickly,” Zhang Chunqiu muttered to himself.</p>
<p>“Doesn’t the Family Clan of Gods also have the Solar Holy Body? Why can’t he be from the Family Clan of Gods?” Zhang Yuzhi asked in puzzlement as she watched the live broadcast.</p>
<p>“The Family Clan of Gods does have the Solar Holy Body from the Sun God Holy Temple, but the Family Clan of Gods doesn’t have that piece of armor he’s wearing. If I’m not wrong, that armor was transformed from a Guardian. Furthermore, it possesses the extremely pure power of the Sun. It’s even purer than the Solar Holy Body’s. I’m afraid only the fellows from the Sun God Holy Temple can create such a Guardian. The Family Clan of Gods doesn’t have it,” Zhang Chunqiu said.</p>
<p>The armor on the Saint from the Sun God Holy Temple emitted a divine solar glow, absorbing the power of the blast.</p>
<p>Under the attention of everyone, the Saint walked to the teleportation nexus and teleported out of Dubhe Palace.</p>
<p>Soon, the Cube’s screen switched to the rankings. It showed a new name. Furthermore, it was ranked ahead of Fire-Armored God—having obtained first place.</p>
<p>“Saint Jiuyang. He’s indeed from the Sun God Holy Temple,” Xia Liuchuan said with a frown.</p>
<p>Upon seeing this name, people realized that this young man was a Saint of the Holy Land.</p>
<p>“The Holy Land is indeed powerful. Any Saint can enter the rankings.”</p>
<p>Humans indeed rely on Guardians.</p>
<p>“That depends on who it is. Our Human Sovereign doesn’t need a Guardian.”</p>
<p>“I’m afraid Human Sovereign can’t enter. Otherwise, why hasn’t he appeared?”</p>
<p>“Aren’t you curious why that Jiuyang can enter the dimensional zone alone?”</p>
<p>No one answered his question. Some thought of a possibility, but it was so cruel that they couldn’t say it out loud.</p>
<p>A human had not only cleared Dubhe Palace, but he had also overtaken the Fire-Armored God, clinching first place. Instantly, he was in the limelight. The entire Federation was discussing Jiuyang.</p>
<p>“Only Saints from the Sun God Holy Temple can pass through Dubhe Palace so easily, right?”</p>
<p>“Jiuyang is too cool.”</p>
<p>“I’m afraid this is another powerhouse at the Human Sovereign level.”</p>
<p>Most people weren’t stingy with their praises. Even Professor Gu, who had always thought negatively, said in a program that Dubhe Palace was a dimensional zone tailor-made for Saint Jiuyang. It was unlikely any human could reach Jiuyang’s level.</p>
<p>If nothing went wrong, Jiuyang might very well obtain first place on the Cube’s rankings.</p>
<h3 id='chapter1544'>Chapter 1544: Humans Who Worship the Devil King</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon </h5>
<p>“Jiuyang, well done.” Xiao looked at Jiuyang who walked out of the Cube and greeted him with a smile.</p>
<p>“That’s no need for compliments. Even a pig can accomplish such a feat while wearing this Solar Holy Armor,” Jiuyang said coldly.</p>
<p>“You can’t say that. There are so many Saints in the Sun God Holy Temple. Only you were chosen to possess it. That’s your strength,” Xiao said.</p>
<p>Jiuyang’s expression didn’t change. “There’s nothing to be happy about. My opponents aren’t them to begin with. I only want to defeat Human Sovereign. Do you think Human Sovereign will appear this time?”</p>
<p>“Probably. Since he claims to be Human Sovereign, he’s not likely to sit back and watch us obtain the Dubhe Companion Beast,” Xiao said.</p>
<p>“That’s good.” After saying that, Jiuyang turned around and left, ignoring Xiao.</p>
<p>Seeing Jiuyang leave, Xiao sighed softly and muttered to himself, “I hope that fellow doesn’t go. Jiuyang and the Guardian on him are practically invincible in a place like Dubhe.”</p>
<p>Zhou Wen, who was grinding, suddenly sneezed. He wiped his nose and muttered to himself, “Ya’er must be missing me. It’s been so long since I went back to visit her. I wonder how she’s doing.”</p>
<p>Before Zhou Wen could find a way to kill Starlord Titan Gate and continue grinding, he heard screams and shouts coming from the city.</p>
<p>What’s happening? Zhou Wen turned his attention and immediately detected a huge snake that was as red as fire in Regretless City. It slithered across the streets and roofs, opened its mouth, and swallowed a human.</p>
<p>This is the Devil Snake they mentioned, right? Zhou Wen immediately thought of the information Grim Demon had previously obtained.</p>
<p>As the snake was at the Terror grade, the humans in Regretless City couldn’t see it after its Terror transformation. They could only be devoured by it.</p>
<p>Many people knelt on the ground and loudly prayed to the Devil King instead of God.</p>
<p>Seeing that the snake still wanted to devour more people, Zhou Wen instant transmitted over. He held the summoned Golden Wyrm Scissors in his hand and snipped the snake into two.</p>
<p>Splash! Splash!</p>
<p>After the snake died, its body exited its Terror form and fell to the ground. Large amounts of snake blood dyed the nearby streets red as though it had just rained blood.</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency… Long live…” When people saw the snake corpse and Zhou Wen floating in the air, they immediately knelt towards him like pious believers, thanking him for saving their lives.</p>
<p>They seemed to be certain that Zhou Wen was Lost Paradise’s Devil King.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen didn’t wish to explain. He searched the snake corpse and found an Essence Energy Crystal.</p>
<p>There are Essence Energy Crystals in dimensional creatures as well? Then, could there be Companion Eggs? Zhou Wen suddenly had the urge to kill all the dimensional bigwigs to see if he could find Companion Eggs.</p>
<p>1</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was just musing. At the very least, he wasn’t in the mood to experiment.</p>
<p>The humans only dared to get up after he returned to the cemetery. They looked at each other with mixed expressions.</p>
<p>…</p>
<p>Not long after Zhou Wen returned to the cemetery—before he could even take out his phone—he saw Grim Demon fly back.</p>
<p>“What happened?” Zhou Wen sized up Grim Demon and couldn’t help but frown when he realized that he was injured in several places.</p>
<p>“I’m fine. That snake didn’t get the better of me either.” Grim Demon recounted his experience.</p>
<p>There was indeed a red snake in the mountain range behind Regretless City. Furthermore, there were many of them. Grim Demon wanted to visit somewhere further away, but after a few roundabouts, he was still discovered by the red snake.</p>
<p>The average red snake was naturally not Grim Demon’s match. Grim Demon even killed those at the same Terror grade. However, when a Calamity-grade red snake appeared, Grim Demon had no choice but to escape.</p>
<p>“These red snakes are extraordinary. They must be related to the legendary Satan. Their bodies are much stronger than the typical creature at the same level,” Grim Demon said.</p>
<p>Just as Zhou Wen was about to say something, he suddenly realized that the elder had arrived outside the cemetery with a few people.</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency… I wish to seek an audience…” the elder said respectfully after knocking on the door.</p>
<p>“What are you doing here?” Zhou Wen walked to the door and opened it.</p>
<p>The elder hurriedly led the humans beside him to kneel and kowtow. After kowtowing, he pointed at the two girls beside him and said, “Your Devilish Excellency, these are the most beautiful girls in our city. I hope you like them.”</p>
<p>“What do you mean?” Zhou Wen looked at the two girls beside the elder. They looked to be about seventeen or eighteen years old. They were extremely beautiful. Their noses were high and their big eyes were deep. They had West District features.</p>
<p>With long brownish-red hair, they exuded a different charm.</p>
<p>What was even more shocking was that the two girls looked identical. They were twins.</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency, you have protected our Regretless City for so many years, preventing us from being harmed by creatures from the outside world. We only wish to repay you. Your Devilish Excellency, you haven’t brought any maids with you. That must be very inconvenient for you. If there’s anything you need, just instruct them…” the elder said.</p>
<p>“There’s no need.” Zhou Wen rejected it immediately. What day and age was it? Humans weren’t inferior to anyone. There was no need for them to kneel to others.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen originally imagined that the two girls would be happy that they didn’t have to serve him, but to his surprise, their faces turned pale when they heard his rejection.</p>
<p>One of the girls rushed forward and hugged Zhou Wen’s calf. “Your Devilish Excellency, please let us follow you. Do as you wish. Leave everything to us. Even if you want us dead, we will be absolutely willing. If you don’t like us, take our lives. We are willing to do anything for you…”</p>
<p>Looking at the sincere girl who looked like a crazy fangirl, Zhou Wen was somewhat speechless.</p>
<p>From the determined looks in the two girls’ eyes, they would immediately commit suicide if Zhou Wen didn’t let them stay.</p>
<p>“Leave the two of them behind. You are dismissed,” Zhou Wen said to the elder.</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency, rest well. I won’t disturb you any further.” Only then did the elder relax. He didn’t dare look up as he kept his head lowered and bowed before leaving the cemetery. He even closed the door behind him.</p>
<p>“What are your names?” Zhou Wen asked as he sized up the two girls.</p>
<p>“I’m Liz. She’s my younger sister, Leem,” the girl who had hugged Zhou Wen’s leg pointed at her sister.</p>
<p>“What can you do?” Zhou Wen asked again.</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency, we can do anything you instruct us to do,” Liz and Leem said at the same time with their heads lowered.. Their cheeks were abnormally red.</p>
<h3 id='chapter1545'>Chapter 1545: The Omniscient Devil King</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon </h5>
<p>“I can get you two to do anything?” Zhou Wen sized up Liz and Leem and asked thoughtfully.</p>
<p>Liz and Leem trembled as their cheeks flushed even redder. Their bodies trembled as they lowered their heads and said, “It’s our honor to be able to offer ourselves to the Devil King.”</p>
<p>Before the two of them came, the City Lord had already explained plenty of things to them. It was because of this that they had such a vivid imagination.</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency, you are the king of Lost Paradise. If we can give birth to Your Devilish Excellency’s son, we can break through the restrictions of the human body and let our descendants reach the Mythical stage. We can fight those gods and devils and no longer be fish on the chopping block. Whether our race can control our fates in the future will be up to you…”</p>
<p>Upon thinking of the City Lord’s serious tone, Liz and Lee couldn’t help but grit their teeth. Although they were still very afraid, they puffed up their chests and displayed their beautiful faces in front of Zhou Wen amidst trembling fear.</p>
<p>“If I were to let you die, would you be willing?” Zhou Wen asked.</p>
<p>He could only use the Cube to return, but four people were needed to enter the Cube. Zhou Wen still needed three, so he was still vexing over the numbers.</p>
<p>Liz and Leem immediately teared up when they heard that. They were extremely afraid. His Devilish Excellency is an omniscient existence. How can our schemes deceive him?</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency, we were wrong. It’s both our fault. It has nothing to do with our clansmen. If you want to punish us, punish us. It doesn’t matter even if you want our lives,” Liz and Leem said as they knelt on the ground and trembled.</p>
<p>“What did you do wrong?” Zhou Wen asked.</p>
<p>“We shouldn’t… shouldn’t have wanted… wanted…” Liz said ‘wanted’ a few times, but she couldn’t continue.</p>
<p>“What do you want?” Zhou Wen asked with a frown. He imagined that the people from Regretless City were secretly plotting to harm him.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was clearly reading too much into it. The people of Regretless City respected the Devil King like a god, so how could they dare harm him?</p>
<p>“We shouldn’t have wanted to use Your Devilish Excellency’s seed…” Leem said through gritted teeth.</p>
<p>Thankfully, Zhou Wen wasn’t drinking water. Otherwise, he would have choked to death. He widened his eyes as he looked at Liz and Leem kneeling in front of him, unable to believe his ears.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen even believed that he had heard wrongly. He wanted them to say it again, but on second thought, it was impossible for him to hear wrongly. It was pointless saying it again. It would only make him feel even more awkward.</p>
<p>“Since you know your mistake, tell me. How should I punish you?” Zhou Wen deliberately asked in a cold manner.</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency, please forgive our clansmen. We are willing to commit suicide to atone for our sins.” Liz and Leem’s faces were filled with determination. They pulled out daggers, hoping to end their lives.</p>
<p>“Did I say I want you two dead?” Zhou Wen’s indifferent voice sounded. Liz and Leem looked at Zhou Wen in surprise, unsure what he meant.</p>
<p>Only now did they realize how capricious the Devil King was. They couldn’t infer anything via common human thought processes. They felt increasingly afraid and uneasy.</p>
<p>“Your lives no longer belong to you from now on,” Zhou Wen said to them.</p>
<p>“Yes, our lives are yours, Your Devilish Excellency.” Liz and Leem immediately knelt.</p>
<p>“Get up. Prepare some food before cleaning up this place.” Zhou Wen kept them because he wanted to use them when he entered the Cube in the future. He didn’t need them for the time being.</p>
<p>However, Zhou Wen was very curious about the food they ate. It was a perfect chance for him to sample it.</p>
<p>Liz and Leem left the cemetery gratefully as though they had been pardoned.</p>
<p>They went back and told the City Lord about the matter. The City Lord and company were so frightened that their faces turned pale and they nearly peed their pants. Only when they heard the whole story did they feel a lot better.</p>
<p>“The Devil King is indeed an omniscient existence. How can he not know my scheme? I nearly harmed all the clansmen in the city… Thankfully, the Devil King gave us a chance… Liz, Leem… Prepare the best food in our city. No matter what, we have to satisfy the Devil King…” After the elder said that, he felt worried. He personally made the preparations and meticulously did everything to perfection. Finally, he handed the finished product to Liz and Leem and got them to take the food into the cemetery.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was grinding when he saw each of them bring in a basin. The basins contained clear water with a few crystalline green leaves soaked in them.</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency, please have your meal.” Liz and Leem knelt in front of Zhou Wen and raised the two basins above their heads.</p>
<p>Are these leaves delicious? Zhou Wen was puzzled, but he still reached out to take a leaf and put it in his mouth to chew a little.</p>
<p>Just one mouthful made Zhou Wen frown. Although the leaf wasn’t terrible, it definitely wasn’t delicious. It tasted similar to the vegetable leaves on Earth.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen didn’t like western food or raw vegetables. He looked at the two sisters and asked, “Do you usually eat this?”</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency, this is a precious leaf of the Jadeite Grass. It’s a very rare and delicious food. It’s very rare to gather it, and it’s impossible for ordinary people to eat it. Only during ceremonies and rituals will everyone get a little…” Liz answered.</p>
<p>“Then what do you usually eat?” Zhou Wen asked again.</p>
<p>“Usually we eat the roots of the stone grass,” Liz answered.</p>
<p>“Bring me the roots of the stone grass.” Zhou Wen really couldn’t imagine that such vegetable-like leaves were the precious food they were talking about. How terrible would the food they usually ate be?</p>
<p>The two sisters were horrified, believing that Zhou Wen wasn’t satisfied with their hospitality and wanted to beg for mercy.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen repeatedly said that he didn’t blame them and got them to retrieve the stone grass’s roots before they left in disbelief.</p>
<p>When they brought the stone grass’s roots over, Zhou Wen found them not bad—the roots were jade-white and were as thick as a finger. They were rather beautiful.</p>
<p>However, when Zhou Wen bit it, he immediately felt a bitter liquid flow into his mouth.</p>
<p>Is this thing edible at all? Zhou Wen suspected that the people of Regretless City were messing with him. How could something even more bitter than bitter melon be the food they usually ate?</p>
<p>However, Zhou Wen roughly scanned the area with Truth Listener and knew that they weren’t lying to him. Most of the people in Regretless City were eating this.</p>
<p>Looking at the trembling sisters, Zhou Wen sighed inwardly. The people in Regretless City have it worse than the people on Earth.</p>
<p>Humans had stood at the top of the food chain for thousands of years on Earth. At the very least, they had experienced enjoyment. These people were at the bottom of the food chain in the dimension. They couldn’t even eat meat, much less have enjoyment. Any dimensional creature was at the Mythical stage. Who could they kill?</p>
<p>“This is for you..” Zhou Wen took out two pieces of bread and threw them at the sisters.</p>
<h3 id='chapter1546'>Chapter 1546: Ancient Snake</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon </h5>
<p>Liz and Leem caught the bread and looked at Zhou Wen in fear. They didn’t know what Zhou Wen had given them.</p>
<p>At Zhou Wen’s gesture, they realized that it was food. When they took a bite, their eyes widened in disbelief.</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency… You… You are too good to us… This is the food of gods and devils, right? You actually rewarded us with the food of gods and devils… Even if we die, we won’t be able to repay your kindness…” Liz and Leem were so touched that tears came to their eyes as they repeatedly thanked him.</p>
<p>How pitiful. They are so touched just from eating bread. If I were to give you two meat buns, wouldn’t you be so touched that your entire family would willingly become servants… Zhou Wen thought.</p>
<p>“Clean up the cemetery after you are done eating.” Zhou Wen returned to the rocking chair he had taken out and continued grinding.</p>
<p>He wanted to give it another try and see if there was a way to bring people in and out alive. These people had suffered terribly. Zhou Wen really couldn’t bear to exchange their lives for his chance to return home.</p>
<p>“Master, we shall take our leave.” Zhou Wen didn’t notice that Liz and Leem addressed him differently.</p>
<p>They couldn’t bear to eat the bread at all. They carefully put it away before cleaning the cemetery. From time to time, they would steal glances at Zhou Wen, who was lying in the rocking chair, gaming.</p>
<p>To them, everything about Zhou Wen was novel and mysterious.</p>
<p>“How naive. They actually sold their lives for two loaves of bread. What a joke,” Grim Demon said with a twitch of his lips.</p>
<p>“There’s nothing funny about it. It’s the same for you Guardians, much less them,” Zhou Wen said.</p>
<p>“Nonsense. How can I be like them?” Grim Demon was immediately displeased.</p>
<p>“How is it different? To them, bread is something they have never had before. Therefore, they will be touched. To you, the rare items that can enhance your strength will also make you work hard. In essence, they are just rare items. There’s no difference,” Zhou Wen said.</p>
<p>“How can it be the same? It’s completely different, alright?” Grim Demon retorted.</p>
<p>“Then tell me. What’s different?” Zhou Wen asked.</p>
<p>“There are many differences. The value of the items is different, and the effects are different…” Grim Demon retorted.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen ignored Grim Demon and continued gaming.</p>
<p>“Why aren’t you saying anything? Are you faking death just because you can’t win the argument? Speak!” Grim Demon circled around Zhou Wen, but Zhou Wen ignored him. He was so anxious that he flew into a rage.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen treated him as air and ignored him.</p>
<p>Grim Demon kept talking in a huff; if he hadn’t realized that he couldn’t beat Zhou Wen, he would have long slapped him.</p>
<p>Suddenly, Zhou Wen frowned and looked up at the sky above the mountain city.</p>
<p>“You worms actually dare to kill my race’s living beings. I originally wanted to raise you as food, but now that you have a death wish, all of you can die.” A sharp and strange eunuch-like voice sounded. On the mountain peak behind Regretless City was a huge red snake. Its body was coiled around the mountain, and its huge head was hanging above Regretless City as it occasionally flicked its tongue.</p>
<p>The snake was massive. Just its head was about half the size of Regretless City.</p>
<p>The humans in the city were alarmed and many of them collapsed to the ground in fright. Such a huge snake only needed one mouthful to devour them all. Running was futile.</p>
<p>“Not good. Why is this fellow here!” Grim Demon was alarmed when he saw the huge snake. He called out to Zhou Wen, hoping to get him to escape.</p>
<p>Grim Demon had previously encountered this huge snake and nearly failed to return.</p>
<p>“Master… Please save our clansmen…” Liz and Leem rushed over and repeatedly kowtowed to Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>“I’ll give you a chance now. You worm-like creatures have no ability to kill my race. Tell me, who killed it? Today, I can spare half of you. I’ll only eat half.” The snake’s voice sounded again.</p>
<p>Everyone was even more alarmed. The snake imagined that these humans would quickly yield and tell it who had killed the ancient snake.</p>
<p>However, although everyone was trembling, no one exposed the culprit. All of them knelt on the ground and prayed in Zhou Wen’s direction as they muttered something about the Devil King.</p>
<p>“It looks like none of you wish to live.” The snake was enraged. It opened its mouth and was about to devour a portion of the humans. They would naturally speak once they felt fear.</p>
<p>However, before the snake could exert its strength, it heard a voice say: “I killed that snake.”</p>
<p>The snake stopped and looked down at the source of the sound.</p>
<p>A human stood on the roof of a stone building. The voice had come from that human.</p>
<p>“A mere human actually dares to lie in front of me. You do seem to have a death wish, and I’ll fulfill your wish,” the snake said as it sucked at Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>A huge suction force sucked everything near Zhou Wen into the snake’s mouth like a tornado.</p>
<p>Liz, Leem, and the nearby humans were swept into the air as they screamed while flying towards the snake’s mouth.</p>
<p>“Master!” Liz and Leem were still shouting, while the others were calling ‘Devil King.’</p>
<p>At this moment, no one exposed Zhou Wen. It was obvious that their fear of the Devil King was above the huge snake.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen extended his hand and beckoned. The Golden Wyrm Scissors transformed into a golden beam of light that slashed at the snake.</p>
<p>The snake never expected a human to have such powerful strength. It was too late by the time it saw the Golden Wyrm Scissors.</p>
<p>Blood spewed out from the snake’s body as it opened its mouth to bite at the Golden Wyrm Scissors, hoping to swallow it.</p>
<p>However, the Golden Wyrm Scissors sliced the snake’s head into two. The blood in the snake’s body immediately flowed down the mountain like a waterfall.</p>
<p>Boom!</p>
<p>The snake’s body also plummeted, just seconds away from crashing into the city.</p>
<p>The snake’s body was even bigger than Regretless City. If it was hit, the entire city would probably be destroyed.</p>
<p>Roar! Tyrant Behemoth was summoned by Zhou Wen. Its huge body stood at the foot of the mountain as it held the snake’s body with its claws, preventing it from falling.</p>
<p>“Long live the Devil King…” The City Lord led everyone to kneel in Zhou Wen’s direction. They naturally regarded Tyrant Behemoth as a devil summoned by Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>From their point of view, as long as the Devil King was in the city, they wouldn’t have to worry about the threat of dimensional creatures in the future. How could there be an existence stronger than the Devil King in the world?</p>
<p>“Master!” Liz and Leem’s eyes glistened as they knelt there and looked at Zhou Wen with adulation.</p>
<h3 id='chapter1547'>Chapter 1547: Devil King’s Food</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon </h5>
<p>Tyrant Behemoth placed the huge snake at the foot of the mountain. Tyrant Behemoth easily tore apart the huge snake after it lost its energy and life.</p>
<p>Not long after, Zhou Wen saw that a portion of the snake’s bones was blood-red and emitted strange energy. It was likely the body of a Calamity-grade creature.</p>
<p>These parts were stored in the Chaos Bead by Zhou Wen. They were good items obtained from a Calamity-grade creature. After advancing to the Calamity grade, he needed such high-energy flesh and bones to replenish his energy. Otherwise, he might really starve to death.</p>
<p>Tsukuyomi and company were examples. After leaving Earth, they had to hunt Calamity creatures to maintain their energy.</p>
<p>Inside the snake’s corpse, he discovered a Companion Egg. It excited Zhou Wen greatly. This was a Calamity-grade Companion Beast—an extremely rare drop.</p>
<p>There was too much snake meat left. Zhou Wen only stored a portion in his chaos space. The rest was used to improve the lives of the people in Regretless City.</p>
<p>Many people here had never eaten meat in their lives. They didn’t even know how to barbecue. It was only when Zhou Wen taught them barbecuing methods that they began eating roasted snake meat.</p>
<p>Just a mouthful of snake meat without any seasoning was sufficient to make many people cry in excitement.</p>
<p>“Long live the Devil King…” Many people praised Zhou Wen as they ate the snake meat.</p>
<p>In the distant valley, a tiny snake peeked its head out from the crack in the mountain. After watching for a while, it burrowed into the mountain and vanished.</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency, this meat is delicious. I left you the best part.” Liz ran over with a bowl of snake meat and offered it to Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>“You can have it.” Calamity-grade snake meat was definitely delicious, but they were like barbarians. They ate it directly after roasting it. Ignoring cumin and chili powder, they didn’t even sprinkle any salt. Zhou Wen wasn’t used to this.</p>
<p>Furthermore, their roasting standards were terrible. Some spots weren’t properly cooked while other spots were charred.</p>
<p>“Your Devilish Excellency, this is specially for you. If Liz were to eat it, she would definitely be cursed to death by everyone.” Leem was much more lively. Although she still respected Zhou Wen, she wasn’t as reserved as before.</p>
<p>Perhaps because he had saved Regretless City, the sisters felt that the Devil King already treated them like family.</p>
<p>“Come over,” Zhou Wen called out to Liz.</p>
<p>Liz came over with a bowl and picked up a piece of snake meat. “Master, let me serve you.”</p>
<p>“Put it on the table.” Zhou Wen was at a loss whether to laugh or cry. This place was too backward. There wasn’t even a knife or fork to eat, much less chopsticks. All they did was grab food with their hands.</p>
<p>Right, all they eat are grass, roots, and leaves. There’s no need for utensils. Zhou Wen thought about it and understood their difficulties.</p>
<p>All Liz could do was place the bowl on the table. Zhou Wen took out his fork and knife and sliced off the parts that weren’t cooked and charred, leaving only a portion that was better roasted.</p>
<p>Then, he took out his barbecue seasonings and sprinkled them on the meat before cutting it into small pieces and slowly eating with chopsticks.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen preferred skewers, but these fellows roasted the meat in large chunks. He could only make do.</p>
<p>Liz and Leem widened their eyes as they watched Zhou Wen. They had never seen anyone eat like Zhou Wen. They felt that the chopsticks were like divine artifacts.</p>
<p>Master is indeed the Devil King. He looks so beautiful and elegant even when eating, Liz thought.</p>
<p>As for Leem, she was in a daze as she looked at the meat. She had an acute sense of smell. The fragrance emitted by the seasoned roasted meat was completely different from the original meat. The smell made Leem’s saliva involuntarily secrete quickly. She couldn’t help but gulp as her stomach rumbled.</p>
<p>They tried roasting meat and when their technique was passable, they immediately delivered Zhou Wen a piece of meat that was better roasted. They hadn’t even had a bite.</p>
<p>“I don’t want to eat this. Eat it. Don’t waste it.” Zhou Wen put down his chopsticks and walked back to his rocking chair. He lay down and took out his phone to check his information.</p>
<p>“Thank you, Master.” Liz and Leem saw that Zhou Wen’s chopsticks and fork were placed there, but they didn’t dare use them. All they did was carefully lift the roasted meat with their hands.</p>
<p>When the roasted meat entered their mouths, they first felt the saltiness from the salt and the spiciness from the chili powder, then the freshness of cumin. Finally, the tender meat and the fragrance of the meat juices seeped out and instantly filled their entire mouths.</p>
<p>This complex taste in the two sisters’ mouths inundated their taste buds. It was an experience they had never had. They felt as though their hearts had melted with this mouthful of roasted meat.</p>
<p>Is this the food the Devil King eats? It’s really delicious. It’s great to be serving the Devil King. Even if I were to die now, I wouldn’t have any regrets. The two girls felt that they had lived all those years in vain.</p>
<p>If Zhou Wen knew what they were thinking, he would probably be at a loss whether to laugh or cry. Just a bit of roasted meat was enough to exchange for two lives. It was as though human lives were worth nothing.</p>
<p>However, Zhou Wen wasn’t in the mood to pay attention to them. He didn’t know what they were thinking either.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was checking Tyrant Behemoth’s stats. The stats after Tyrant Behemoth’s evolution didn’t exceed Zhou Wen’s expectations.</p>
<p>Tyrant Behemoth: Calamity (Evolvable)</p>
<p>Life Providence: Extreme Strength, Mountain River Absorption</p>
<p>Life Soul: Violent Crown</p>
<p>Wheel of Destiny: Absolute Strength (S-grade)</p>
<p>Terror Form: Tyrant</p>
<p>Calamity Zone: Overlord Zone (Human Realm)</p>
<p>Strength: 100</p>
<p>Speed: 100</p>
<p>Constitution: 100</p>
<p>Essence Energy: 100</p>
<p>Talent Skill: Mountain Consuming, Rampage, Behemoth, Armor Breaker, Penetration, Ripping, Poison Fang, Bite, Ever-Victorious, Unstoppable.</p>
<p>Companion Form: Boxing Glove</p>
<p>The stats and skills were within Zhou Wen’s expectations. He mainly wanted to see what the Calamity Zone was. From the introduction, the Overlord Zone was likely a domain that enhanced strength.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen didn’t study it too much. He would slowly experiment when he had the chance in the future. Now, what Zhou Wen mainly wanted to study was the huge snake Companion Egg.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen had already stored the Companion Egg in-game and checked its stats.</p>
<p>Ancient Snake: Calamity</p>
<p>Life Providence: Devil</p>
<p>Life Soul: Snake Devil</p>
<p>Wheel of Destiny: Devil’s Tongue (S-grade)</p>
<p>Terror Form: Blood Shadow</p>
<p>Calamity Zone: Temptation Zone (Hell-level)</p>
<p>Strength: 278</p>
<p>Speed: 267</p>
<p>Constitution: 245</p>
<p>Essence Energy: 232</p>
<p>Talent Skill: Whale Devouring, Poison Fangs, Rend</p>
<p>Companion Form: Staff</p>
<p>Zhou Wen carefully studied the Ancient Snake’s information and realized that it was a surprising Companion Beast. This was the first time he had seen a staff as a companion form.</p>
<p>Previously, he had heard that there were magic staff-type Companion Beasts in the West District. The magic staff itself came with magical spells.</p>
<p>However, the staff formed by the Ancient Snake was still somewhat different from ordinary magic staffs.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen didn’t think much of the Ancient Snake’s skill, but its Calamity Zone seemed rather interesting.</p>
<h3 id='chapter1548'>Chapter 1548: Accidental Kill</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon </h5>
<p>Legend has it that Satan transformed into an ancient snake and lured Adam and Eve into depravity. Is the Temptation Zone of this Ancient Snake related to that legend? Zhou Wen guessed.</p>
<p>To know the exact effects of the Temptation Zone, he had to give it a try. Zhou Wen hatched the Ancient Snake and summoned it in its staff form.</p>
<p>A snake-headed staff appeared in Zhou Wen’s hand. It was about two meters long. The head of the staff was a snake’s head, and its end was a snake’s tail. In the middle was a coiled snake’s body that was as red as blood. Its eyes were like two rubies that shimmered with a demonic glow. It looked extremely bizarre.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen waved it a few times and injected Essence Energy into it, but he realized that the staff didn’t have any long-range attacks or any spells.</p>
<p>What kind of crappy staff is this? Is it expecting a mage to use a staff like a daibo? Will that make me a mage or a warrior? Zhou Wen thought to himself.</p>
<p>He entered a dungeon in-game with the Ancient Snake and allowed it to take form. A huge ancient snake appeared in front of Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>With such a huge body, it was definitely powerful in melee combat. However, what Zhou Wen wanted to know wasn’t its melee abilities, but the capabilities of its domain.</p>
<p>Dimensional creatures rushed towards Zhou Wen. Although the dimensional creatures were low-level creatures without even a single Mythical creature, Zhou Wen still got the Ancient Snake to use its domain as a test of its abilities.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen originally imagined that a Companion Beast like the Ancient Snake would cause quite a stir when it released its domain, but to his surprise, it didn’t have any lighting effects. All he heard was a faint sound coming from the Ancient Snake’s mouth. Although it wasn’t loud, it was like the murmur of a devil. It left Zhou Wen vexed.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen just felt frustrated. The other dimensional creatures that approached the Ancient Snake seemed to go mad as they fought each other. The scene devolved into pandemonium.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was overjoyed. Clearly, the Temptation Zone was a domain that could throw the enemy into disarray. It could even make the enemy kill each other. This reminded Zhou Wen of the dimensional creature on Merak Star. Its sound-type ability made the Golden Wyrm Scissors switch sides. There seemed to be some similarities.</p>
<p>He walked deeper into the dungeon with the Ancient Snake. This feeling was indeed great. There was no need for him to do it himself as the dimensional creatures began fighting themselves. He felt like a god playing with life.</p>
<p>However, the Temptation Zone wasn’t invincible. Zhou Wen attempted to get the Ancient Snake to use the Temptation Zone on him, but it was useless. All it did was pressure him mentally.</p>
<p>The creature on Merak seems to have similar abilities, but the effects are stronger than the Ancient Snake’s Temptation Zone. I wonder if using the Ancient Snake’s Temptation Zone can resist Starlord Titan Gate’s strength.</p>
<p>With this in mind, Zhou Wen immediately launched the Big Dipper instance dungeon. Starlord Ravenous Wolf of the Dubhe Palace hadn’t respawned, so Zhou Wen went straight to the Merak Star Palace and faced Starlord Titan Gate again.</p>
<p>Starlord Titan Gate let out another terrifying roar as a powerful shockwave surged over. Zhou Wen summoned the Golden Wyrm Scissors and the Ancient Snake while he protected himself with the Chaos Egg.</p>
<p>The Golden Wyrm Scissors went against the sound wave, but the Ancient Snake stayed in place. It flicked its tongue, letting out a strange murmur.</p>
<p>The Ancient Snake’s murmurs weren’t lethal. Starlord Titan Gate’s roar vanished upon clashing with the murmurs. It was almost inaudible.</p>
<p>The Ancient Snake had thick skin and flesh, so it could temporarily withstand it. What Zhou Wen was most worried about was the Golden Wyrm Scissors flying back and attacking him ruthlessly.</p>
<p>Strangely, nothing like that happened. The Golden Wyrm Scissors quickly rushed over and chopped off Starlord Titan Gate’s head with one strike.</p>
<p>‘Killed Starlord Titan Gate. Discovered Dimensional Crystal.’</p>
<p>He died just like that? Zhou Wen found it unbelievable.</p>
<p>Starlord Titan Gate only dropped two stat crystals—there were no Companion Eggs. It left Zhou Wen somewhat disappointed.</p>
<p>However, killing Starlord Titan Gate was already a pleasant surprise. He couldn’t demand any more.</p>
<p>The Golden Wyrm Scissors is really useful. As long as it can get close, it can slice apart anything at the same level. Zhou Wen’s fondness for the Golden Wyrm Scissors increased.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen had also attempted the Venusian instance dungeon. He was killed by the strange artifact every time. Up to now, Zhou Wen didn’t know what the artifact was, nor had he won once.</p>
<p>It was useless even if he had the Hell-level Golden Wyrm Scissors. He died the same way.</p>
<p>After feeding the stat crystal to the Companion Beast, Zhou Wen arrived at the back of the Merak Star Palace. Indeed, there was a teleportation nexus there.</p>
<p>Without any hesitation, Zhou Wen chose to head to the third star, Phecda.</p>
<p>There was little information about Phecda. It wasn’t as famous as Dubhe and Merak. Zhou Wen only knew its name, but he wasn’t too sure about its legends.</p>
<p>Phecda Star Palace wasn’t as exaggerated as the Merak Star Palace. It looked like an ordinary temple on Earth.</p>
<p>Opening the door to Phecda Star Palace, he saw a person in green armor inside. Zhou Wen only remembered Phecda, but he couldn’t recall the corresponding Starlord’s name.</p>
<p>Regardless of what Starlord the other party was, Zhou Wen only had one set of moves. He used the Golden Wyrm Scissors and the Ancient Snake’s Temptation Zone.</p>
<p>The green-armored Starlord didn’t seem to be as ferocious as Starlord Ravenous Wolf and Starlord Titan Gate. When the Golden Wyrm Scissors flew over, he didn’t seem to react at all.</p>
<p>Crack!</p>
<p>The green-armored Starlord was sliced into two by the Golden Wyrm Scissors. Zhou Wen imagined that he had successfully passed the test and could head to the next Star Palace when he heard a crack. The Golden Wyrm Scissors had snapped.</p>
<p>How did that happen? Zhou Wen was alarmed. The Golden Wyrm Scissors was one of the strongest at the Hell level. Even a Heaven-level creature would find it difficult to snap it.</p>
<p>Furthermore, Zhou Wen didn’t discover anything lunging at the Golden Wyrm Scissors. It looked like it had snapped on its own.</p>
<p>Thankfully, it was in-game. Otherwise, it would have been a huge loss if the Golden Wyrm Scissors had snapped.</p>
<p>As for the green-armored Starlord that had been sliced into two, his body strangely recovered when the Golden Wyrm Scissors snapped as though he had never been injured.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen’s heart palpitated as he got the Ancient Snake to charge over.</p>
<p>The Ancient Snake’s Temptation Zone didn’t seem to be of much use to the green-armored Starlord. He stood there without being affected. The Ancient Snake bit down and swallowed him.</p>
<p>The tiny body of the green-armored Starlord wasn’t even enough to fill the gaps between the Ancient Snake’s teeth.</p>
<p>Before Zhou Wen could rejoice, the Ancient Snake’s massive body suddenly shrank rapidly. The green-armored Starlord appeared out of thin air from the Ancient Snake’s body. Instead, it opened its mouth wide and swallowed the now minified Ancient Snake.</p>
<p>What’s going on? What’s wrong with this fellow? Zhou Wen was dumbfounded.</p>
<h3 id='chapter1549'>Chapter 1549: Something’s Not Right</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon </h5>
<p>The green-armored Starlord stood there without any intention of taking the initiative to attack. He stared coldly at the blood-colored avatar as though he was saying: “Didn’t you want to kill me? Bring it on.”</p>
<p>Zhou Wen summoned Bamboo Blade and slashed at the green-armored Starlord.</p>
<p>The green-armored Starlord didn’t dodge. He stood there, allowing Zhou Wen free rein to slash at him.</p>
<p>The Bamboo Blade in Zhou Wen’s hand was as fast as lightning as he slashed at the green-armored Starlord repeatedly. With the Bamboo Blade’s destructive power and Zhou Wen’s strength, he had strength equivalent to the Calamity grade.</p>
<p>He only left scuffs on the armor after slashing more than a hundred times. He failed to really injure the green-armored Starlord.</p>
<p>Wounds appeared on Zhou Wen’s body one after another. The spot where his body was injured was where the Bamboo Blade had left a saber mark on the green-armored Starlord.</p>
<p>Bang!</p>
<p>Just as Zhou Wen stopped his saber, the green-armored Starlord suddenly punched the blood-colored avatar, killing it. The game screen went black.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen didn’t immediately enter the game again. Instead, he closed his eyes to recall the battle.</p>
<p>The power of the green-armored Starlord appears reflective, but it’s definitely not as simple as a reflection. No matter how strong a reflection is, it’s impossible for him to identically transfer his injuries to someone else… The more Zhou Wen thought about it, the more excited he became.</p>
<p>He liked such novel dungeons. It was very boring to always grind repetitive dungeons.</p>
<p>He failed to figure out the problem despite plenty of thinking. All he could do was continue grinding dungeons.</p>
<p>He didn’t know how many times he tried, but the outcome was the same. No matter what kind of attack hit the green-armored Starlord, the injuries would return to him. It was unbelievable.</p>
<p>He came up with all sorts of methods. He could only defend without attacking; otherwise, just injuring the green-armored Starlord would doom him.</p>
<p>It was useless to blindly send himself to his death again and again, so Zhou Wen decided not to grind the Big Dipper instance dungeon. He switched to other dungeons to change his train of thought.</p>
<p>However, even if he couldn’t kill the green-armored Starlord, Zhou Wen still had a chance of returning home. He was probably the only one on Earth who could kill two Starlords in a row.</p>
<p>“Master, here’s your roasted meat.” Leem delivered roasted meat during meal time.</p>
<p>“You can have it.” Zhou Wen had been having a lot of roasted meat recently and was sick of it. He really couldn’t force himself to eat it.</p>
<p>“That’s not too nice, right? This is for you, Master,” Leem said.</p>
<p>“I told you to eat it. Do you dare say no? Just eat it in peace,” Zhou Wen said indifferently.</p>
<p>“Thank you, Master.” Although Leem said that, she didn’t eat the roasted meat. She continued looking at Zhou Wen eagerly.</p>
<p>When Zhou Wen saw Leem’s expression, he immediately understood what she was up to. He took out some seasonings and handed them to her. “Sprinkle them yourself.”</p>
<p>“Thank you for the reward, Master.” Leem held the seasoning bottles and was so excited that she nearly couldn’t say a word.</p>
<p>Humans here are easily satisfied. When they come into contact with the flourishing Earth, I’m afraid there won’t be such simple happiness, Zhou Wen thought.</p>
<p>Leem took the seasonings and ran to Liz. The two of them sprinkled seasonings on the roasted meat and ate until their mouths were covered in oil.</p>
<p>You’re at the Epic stage after all. There’s no need for you to eat so messily. Zhou Wen shook his head with a wistful smile.</p>
<p>Suddenly, Zhou Wen realized something. He looked at Liz and Leem again. Something’s amiss. Liz and Leem are at the Epic stage. To be able to reach the Epic stage at their age means they are extremely impressive geniuses based on my experience on Earth. But how did they advance to the Epic stage?</p>
<p>The humans in Regretless City were too weak, so weak that Zhou Wen didn’t even realize a problem with them.</p>
<p>However, on careful thought, most of the humans in the city were at the Legendary stage. There were also quite a number of Epic experts, but how had they advanced?</p>
<p>There were no low-level dimensional creatures in a place like Regretless City. The weakest dimensional creature outside was at the Mythical stage, but Regretless City couldn’t even find a single Mythical creature. How could they hunt?</p>
<p>“Liz, let me ask you something. You need to answer truthfully,” Zhou Wen called her over and asked.</p>
<p>“I’ll answer anything, Master,” Liz hurriedly said.</p>
<p>“How do the humans in your city advance all the way from the Mortal stage? What tools do they usually use?</p>
<p>“What does advancing mean?” Liz asked in puzzlement.</p>
<p>“Do you know about Life Providences and Life Souls?” Zhou Wen asked after some thought.</p>
<p>“Yes, isn’t that something that comes with birth? There’s no need to advance,” Liz answered.</p>
<p>“You have them from birth? Are you sure?” This time, Zhou Wen was truly excited. It was unimaginably simple. Humans here were born at the Legendary or Epic stage.</p>
<p>“Of course I’m sure. Everyone in our city has a Life Providence after being born. Some stronger children will even have a Life Soul at birth,” Liz said after some thought.</p>
<p>How did these fellows do it? From the looks of it, I have to investigate. Zhou Wen decided to figure out why the people in Regretless City received such treatment.</p>
<p>“Liz, what’s your Life Providence and Life Soul?” Zhou Wen asked her first.</p>
<p>Liz and Leem walked over. Upon hearing Zhou Wen ask them, they explained their Life Providences and Life Soul abilities in detail.</p>
<p>The more Zhou Wen listened, the more alarmed he became. Their Life Providences and Life Souls were very special. They were better than the Life Providences and Life Souls of many humans on Earth.</p>
<p>“Get the City Lord over.” Seeing that Liz and Leem couldn’t explain it clearly, Zhou Wen planned on summoning someone useful over. Perhaps he could explain it clearly.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen learned some useful information from the City Lord.</p>
<p>It was said that the humans in Regretless City were indeed very weak in the past, but as time passed, they slowly became stronger.</p>
<p>In the past, babies born were very normal. They were all at the Mortal stage, but over the generations, babies born in Regretless City now had extremely powerful abilities at the Legendary stage. There were even terrifying existences at the Epic stage.</p>
<p>The City Lord couldn’t explain the exact reason.</p>
<p>“I had a few guesses before, but I couldn’t confirm them,” the City Lord said after some thought.</p>
<p>“Share them with me.” Zhou Wen was now very interested in these things.</p>
<p>“There are three reasons according to legend. One is that because we often eat grass roots, they improve our physiques and make us better.”</p>
<p>“What about the second?” Zhou Wen felt that this theory wasn’t reliable. He had recently tried everything they ate. There was nothing special about the grass roots. They weren’t even considered ordinary dimensional plants. At most, they were considered mutated plants.</p>
<p>“The second theory is related to a treasure in Regretless City. Legend has it that there’s a treasure buried there.. Two ancestors brought it out of the Garden of Eden,” the City Lord said after some hesitation.</p>
<h3 id='chapter1550'>Chapter 1550: Treasure Hunting in Regretless City</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon </h5>
<p>A treasure from the Garden of Eden? Zhou Wen frowned in thought.</p>
<p>Legend has it that Adam and Eve were banished from the Garden of Eden because they secretly ate the forbidden fruit. What could they have taken out of the Garden of Eden? The forbidden fruit? This was the only thing Zhou Wen could think of.</p>
<p>However, there were definitely many good things in the Garden of Eden. If they took something else along the way, it wouldn’t be something Zhou Wen could guess.</p>
<p>Regretless City looks very ordinary, but it has evilness lurking in it. There are two puppets in Adam and Eve’s tombs. It also said that there’s some treasure buried under the city that allows humans to have Life Providences and Life Souls. This place is really odd, Zhou Wen thought to himself.</p>
<p>The City Lord stole a glance at Zhou Wen and said cowardly, “There’s also a third guess. It’s said that this place is protected by your magical power, allowing us to have everything we have now. I believe that this is the truth. Everything we have is given to us by you, Your Devilish Excellency.”</p>
<p>“Alright, you may leave.” After Zhou Wen sent the City Lord away, he thought about what he had said.</p>
<p>The third possibility wasn’t high, and the first was even more ridiculous. Zhou Wen had also eaten the roots of the stone grass. They were the roots of ordinary plants. Even if they had any effects, they could at best be treated as herbs. It was impossible to use them to evolve humans to such significance.</p>
<p>The second possibility was most likely. However, Zhou Wen was very interested in what treasures lay beneath Regretless City. He wanted to know what kind of treasure could make humans have such a high starting point.</p>
<p>How can I find it? Zhou Wen planned on trying.</p>
<p>Truth Listener’s ability was very strong. It could even pass through a thick mountain and hear a cave’s interior. However, beneath Regretless City was just pure mountain. There were no caves.</p>
<p>Since the item isn’t in the mountain body, the most likely possibility is that it’s in Regretless City. Zhou Wen used Truth Listener to constantly scan the area, not missing out on any detail, hoping to find some clues.</p>
<p>Buildings in Regretless City had rather interesting styles. There were all sorts of statues, carvings, and murals. Zhou Wen repeatedly scanned them, but he didn’t discover any power that could allow humans to evolve.</p>
<p>Could it be that the treasure in Regretless City is related to the two puppets? After some thought, Zhou Wen realized that the most mysterious thing in Regretless City was likely the two puppets.</p>
<p>If it was really because of the two puppets, Zhou Wen really didn’t dare dig them out. Grim Demon’s lesson was still fresh in his mind. Who knew what strange things would happen if he got the two puppets out?</p>
<p>However, Zhou Wen wasn’t willing to give up just like that. Now that he was establishing a city in Guide City, if there was really such a treasure, it would bring unimaginable benefits if he buried it in his city.</p>
<p>Ignoring the improvements of newborns, just advertising the effects would bring Zhou Wen huge benefits.</p>
<p>Which parent didn’t want their descendants to gain an early advantage? Who didn’t want their children to be better than others? The stronger one was, the stronger their descendants would be.</p>
<p>When they learned that the children in Zhou Wen’s city were born at the Legendary or even Epic stage, how many people would rack their brains to come up with ways to enter his city to have babies?</p>
<p>Just this point alone was sufficient for Zhou Wen to gather a large number of human experts. Even if those human experts weren’t willing to join Zhou Wen’s city, he could take the opportunity to earn large amounts of benefits. He could even exchange for resources that couldn’t be obtained with money.</p>
<p>In short, with this treasure, it was impossible for Zhou Wen not to develop his city.</p>
<p>The crux of the matter was how to find this treasure. Also, he had to find a safe place to build a city and prevent easy entry.</p>
<p>I’ll do a search first. If there aren’t any treasures, it’s useless no matter how much I fantasize. Zhou Wen pondered for a moment and took out a tiny beast from the chaos space.</p>
<p>The little beast looked like a cross between a ferret and a rat, with a squirrel-like tail. It looked very strange.</p>
<p>The origins of this little beast were not simple. Previously, Tai Sui was bitten out of the metal walnut by this little beast. Furthermore, it could replicate a weapon like the Orchid Blade with identical material and effects. It was very magical.</p>
<p>Back when Zhou Wen obtained this little beast, he had kept it in the chaos space. His subsequent research on its origins came up to nothing.</p>
<p>However, Zhou Wen knew the beast’s abilities very well. It had a rare Earth Escape technique and was good at finding treasures.</p>
<p>Now, Zhou Wen had no choice but to try using it.</p>
<p>After all, he had raised it for so many years. This little beast’s feral nature had decreased dramatically. It was considered close to Zhou Wen, but it was a little too cunning. Zhou Wen wasn’t too confident in its loyalty.</p>
<p>The moment the little beast came out, it looked around furtively. Perhaps because it hadn’t come out for a long time, it felt a little uncomfortable and appeared a little reserved.</p>
<p>However, after it sized up its surroundings, it gradually revealed its true nature and peeked everywhere.</p>
<p>“There’s a treasure in this city. If you can find it, we’ll split the treasure equally. In addition, I’ll give you a Mythical Companion Egg as a reward.” Zhou Wen first promised the little beast benefits.</p>
<p>The little beast wasn’t his Companion Beast, nor was it as loyal as Chick. It was difficult to entice it without offering some benefits.</p>
<p>Upon hearing Zhou Wen’s words, the little beast stood up like a human and gestured at him with its two tiny paws.</p>
<p>Its actions were very simple. It extended its claws and flipped back and forth several times.</p>
<p>“You want twenty? Isn’t that a little too greedy? My final offer is two,” Zhou Wen said.</p>
<p>However, the little beast was very insistent. It waved its claws and gestured twenty again. It refused to give in at all.</p>
<p>“Three… Four… Five… Ten…” Zhou Wen kept raising the price, but the little beast was very willful. It didn’t lower its asking price at all. It kept at twenty.</p>
<p>“Fine, twenty it is. However, the thing you find has to be the one I want. You can’t randomly find something to fool me,” Zhou Wen said.</p>
<p>The little beast nodded and looked around for a while. It sniffed the air and ran off in a certain direction.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen hurriedly followed the little beast and watched it sniff around. It looked like a police hound.</p>
<p>After leaving the cemetery, the people on the streets immediately prostrated themselves at the ‘Devil King’ when they saw Zhou Wen. Wherever Zhou Wen went, people knelt on the ground, making him uncomfortable.</p>
<p>The little beast didn’t care much. It circled the city randomly.. After circling for a while, it actually headed for a cliff.</p>
<h3 id='chapter1551'>Chapter 1551: Digging Up a Treasure</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon </h5>
<p>Zhou Wen came from the cliff—across the cliff was Lost Paradise. He had previously observed the cliff and didn’t discover anything amiss.</p>
<p>However, the little beast ran firmly towards the edge of the cliff, leaving Zhou Wen somewhat puzzled. Could it be that the treasure is at the bottom of the cliff?</p>
<p>Soon, Zhou Wen dispelled this thought because the little beast stopped by the cliff and sniffed a stone.</p>
<p>Could it be that there’s something wrong with that stone? Zhou Wen’s mind locked onto the stone, but he didn’t discover any problems. It was as though it was a very ordinary mountain rock that was no different from the stones beside it.</p>
<p>“It looks like this little fellow of yours isn’t very reliable,” Grim Demon said.</p>
<p>The tiny beast seemed to understand him. It bared its teeth at Grim Demon and squealed as though it was cursing him. Zhou Wen didn’t even have the chance to answer.</p>
<p>“You can see me?” Grim Demon was slightly taken aback. He was in his Terror form, so it was impossible for others to see him without reaching the Terror grade.</p>
<p>This little beast’s level was clearly very low. It was impossible for it to be at the Terror grade. For it to see Grim Demon left him incredulous.</p>
<p>The little beast continued squealing at him, clearly able to see him.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen wasn’t in the mood to care about them. He walked to the stone and carefully sized it up. The stone was likely an ordinary mountain rock, but there was something very strange.</p>
<p>The area around the cliff was a platform. The other parts were flat. Only this stone protruded a foot tall and its surface was very smooth from the weathering.</p>
<p>“You, come over.” Zhou Wen called out to a person kneeling not far away and asked, “Why is there a protruding stone here?”</p>
<p>The person thought for a moment and answered, “Your Devilish Excellency, this stone has been here for a long time. I don’t know when it appeared because it’s on the edge of the cliff. We usually tie a rope around it and use the rope to go down the cliff to find some edible plants and fungi.”</p>
<p>“Call your City Lord over,” Zhou Wen instructed when he saw that he couldn’t get much from him.</p>
<p>Not long after, the elder jogged over. After meeting him, he knelt again.</p>
<p>“Enough, stop prostrating. Tell me, when did this stone appear here?” Zhou Wen waved his hand to stop the elder from kneeling.</p>
<p>He wasn’t used to such etiquette to begin with, and it was a waste of time.</p>
<p>Only then did the elder stand properly and say, “Your Devilish Excellency, I’ve only heard from the elders that there was a monument erected here before Regretless City was established. As my elders didn’t know who erected it here, they didn’t dare to randomly remove it. Nothing special came out of this monument over time; therefore, from my elders onwards, they used this monument as a pillar, tying ropes to it to aid our descent to search for food.”</p>
<p>The elder paused for a moment before continuing, “Much later, due to the elements and a few accidents, the stone monument snapped. Later on, it underwent a few problems, leaving only this tiny piece in our generation. We aren’t too sure of its origins.”</p>
<p>A stone monument? Zhou Wen frowned as he looked at the protruding stone that was a foot tall. It was very difficult to associate it with a stone monument.</p>
<p>Furthermore, this monument had actually shattered. If it was really that magical, how could it shatter so easily?</p>
<p>The people from Regretless City didn’t know much about the stone. Zhou Wen waved his hand and dismissed them.</p>
<p>The tiny beast ran in front of Zhou Wen and extended its claws. From the looks of it, it was asking Zhou Wen for its Companion Eggs.</p>
<p>This fellow was like a weasel, but what it liked to eat wasn’t chicken eggs, but Companion Eggs. It loved eating the higher-level ones.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen had previously fed it quite a number of Companion Eggs. Although their levels weren’t high and most of them were at the Epic stage, it hadn’t evolved over the years.</p>
<p>“Are you sure this stone is a treasure?” Zhou Wen asked the little beast.</p>
<p>The little beast pointed at the stone with its claws and made another digging motion.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen immediately understood that the treasure wasn’t the stone, but beneath it.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen summoned Tyrant Behemoth and got it to dig up the stone. It was most suitable for such manual labor.</p>
<p>Tyrant Behemoth didn’t transform into its huge form. It shrank to a height of four to five meters, extended its claws, and swiped down, slicing open the stone like tofu.</p>
<p>After moving its claws a few times, the protruding rock was dug out completely, leaving a hole more than a meter deep.</p>
<p>Clang!</p>
<p>Tyrant Behemoth’s claws seemed to touch something as they emitted a metallic clang.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen hurriedly walked over and looked into the pit. He realized that there was a green metal object. It looked like a bronze artifact.</p>
<p>He summoned Bamboo Blade and removed the rocks beside the bronze artifact. Soon, the bronze artifact was completely exposed.</p>
<p>What’s this? Zhou Wen sized up the bronze artifact that had been taken out of the pit, but after looking at it for a while, he couldn’t figure out what it was.</p>
<p>This item looked very strange. Zhou Wen had never seen such a bronze artifact.</p>
<p>Typical bronze tools, such as tripod cauldrons, furnaces, and spoons were nothing to speak of. Even some unknown bronze artifacts looked somewhat similar.</p>
