<h3 id='chapter1581'>Chapter 1581: Nondisputatious Sword Intent</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>
<p>Sincere words are not fine; fine words are not sincere.</p>
<p>Those who are skilled do not dispute; the disputatious are not skilled in it.</p>
<p>Those who know are not extensively learned; the extensively learned do not know it.</p>
<p>The sage does not accumulate for himself. The more that he expends for others, the more does he possess of his own; the more that he gives to others, the more does he have himself.</p>
<p>With all the sharpness of the Way of Heaven, it injures not; with all the doing in the way of the sage he does not strive.</p>
<p>This was the origin of the Nondisputatious Sword Intent. It was a passage from ancient scriptures.</p>
<p>The skilled didn’t need to strive. Things would naturally fall into their hands because others couldn’t do what they could do. It would only be natural for the things to be given to them.</p>
<p>Jiuyang’s realm also contained this concept. He pursued his own cultivation without being affected by anything else.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen looked at Jiuyang’s realm and gained a deeper understanding of the Nondisputatious Sword Intent.</p>
<p>3000 sword intents are just too many. If I want to figure out the true meaning of all of them, forget a mortal like me with about a hundred years of lifespan, even if I could live for more than a thousand years and figure out one every year, that will only cover a third. Besides, it’s impossible for me to figure</p>
<p>out the true meaning of one sword intent in a year. I’s fine if I just figure out a few things in the fature, but I can’t pursue perfection like Jiuyang. The ancient scripture’s saying is right. Those who know are not extensively learned; the extensively learned do not know it. Although my 3,000 sword intents</p>
<p>aren’t weak, Jiuyang’s realm is much higher than any of the 3,000 sword intents, Zhou Wen thought.</p>
<p>As the essence of their realms were too similar, Zhou Wen quickly made a huge breakthrough in the Nondisputatious Sword Intent from referencing Jiuyang.</p>
<p>Til give it a try and see how well I’ve cultivated this sword intent. Zhou Wen’s saber stance changed as he used a concept similar to Jiuyang’s. It was none other than the Nondisputatious Sword Intent that had just experienced a breakthrough.</p>
<p>Jiuyang,Carlos, and Shenluo’s eyes focused at the same time. They could tell that the change in Zhou Wen’s saber aura was very similar to Jiuyang’s boxing concept.</p>
<p>He actually wants to imitate Jiuyang’s technique and concept. Isn’t he a little too idealistic? How can such a realm be mastered in a short period of time? It’s especially so for Jiuyang’s characteristic of pursuing details. It’s not something that can be mastered just from mimicking. He’s aiming high only to</p>
<p>achieve little. Shenluo snorted coldly.</p>
<p>Carlos was also somewhat puzzled. Zhou Wen’s actions seemed a little too rash.</p>
<p>It was true that Zhou Wen was a genius, but Jiuyang was also a genius. Furthermore, he was a top genius. To use Jiuyang’s ultimate skill that he had cultivated for so many years after such a short period of time was a little arrogant.</p>
<p>However, the battle left the two dumbfounded.</p>
<p>‘The saber in Zhou Wen’s hand remained sheathed, but he had already switched from defense to offense. During the battle with Jiuyang, the similarity of their techniques and realms exceeded 90%.</p>
<p>More importantly, Zhou Wen had managed to tie with Jiuyang without being at a disadvantage.</p>
<p>“Could it be that… there’s really such a genius in this world…” Carlos widened his eyes and muttered to himself in disbelief.</p>
<p>“What do you mean?” By the side, Youkai didn’t understand. He could only tell that Zhou Wen wasn’t blindly defending, but his attacks weren’t very powerful. They were very ordinary.</p>
<p>Carlos said with a bitter smile, “Youkai, do you think I’m considered a genius?”</p>
<p>“Of course. If you aren’t a genius, there aren’t any geniuses in the Federation. Although you don’t have the Sovereign Body inherited from your family, your talent and comprehension far exceed those fellows with the Sovereign Body. I still remember the time when you trained in an Essence Energy Skill</p>
<p>John took two months to master. You did it for a short while to be much stronger than him,” said Youkai.</p>
<p>“Then, do you think it’s possible for someone to learn something that will take me one to two decades in just a few minutes?”</p>
<p>“That’s naturally impossible. A human who can do such a thing, no—I shouldn’t say human; it’s impossible for humans to do it. If they can do it, they are not human at all,” said Youkai.</p>
<p>“But that fellow just did it,” said Carlos with another bitter smile.</p>
<p>“Who? What did he do?” Youkai was stunned and asked blankly.</p>
<p>“Jiuyang’s talent isn’t inferior to mine. I believe his cultivation realm was obtained through arduous cultivation. If it were me, I would also need so much time, but in the short twenty to thirty minutes of battle, Zhou Wen actually reached the same realm as him. He’s even on par with Jiuyang,” said Carlos.</p>
<p>“That’s impossible, right? Could it be that Zhou Wen already knew it and is only using it now?” Youkai guessed with a look of disbelief.</p>
<p>Carlos sighed and said, “I hope so too, but it’s obvious that his realm is still improving. He should still be in the midst of comprehension. In the past, I always felt that I was a genius, not inferior to anyone in the Federation. Even An Tianzuo was only a target for me to catch up with in my studies.</p>
<p>However, after meeting Zhou Wen today, I suddenly feel disheartened and even some despair.”</p>
<p>“Don’t think that way. There must be a reason. It’s impossible for there to be such a genius among humans. There must be a problem. We can find the problem. Don’t give up…” Youkai immediately panicked. Carlos was the most promising person in the Cape family now. If he were to be dispirited, it would</p>
<p>undoubtedly be a fatal blow to the Cape family.</p>
<p>“Don’t worry. I’m not a greenhouse flower who hasn’t experienced storms. Even if Zhou Wen is really such a genius, I won’t give up on my goal. I’m just feeling wistful.”</p>
<p>“That’s good.” Youkai heaved a sigh of relief when he saw that there was nothing abnormal about the latter’s expression. However, he was still alarmed.</p>
<p>If it was really as Carlos had said, Zhou Wen was too terrifying.</p>
<p>Shenluo’s surprise was far greater than that of the two. They didn’t know much about Jiuyang, so they were only speculating.</p>
<p>However, Shenluo knew a lot about Jiuyang. Among the many Saints in the Sun God Holy Temple, only Jiuyang had obtained the recognition of the Sun God Guardian and obtained the Sun God Holy Temple’s Holy Artifact.</p>
<p>Although everyone was a Saint in name, Jiuyang, who controlled the Sun God Holy Temple’s Holy Artifact, was actually the Sun God Temple’s Holy Son.</p>
<p>Shenluo was in a similar situation. He knew very well how great the price one needed to pay to become the Holy Son who controlled the Holy Artifact.</p>
<p>Jiuyang had been cultivating arduously since he was young. His achievements were the result of years of hard work. Even Shenluo had to admit that he was no match for Jiuyang in terms of the martial arts realm.</p>
<p>It was very difficult to mimic Jiuyang’s realm because it wasn’t as simple as hard work. It also required inhuman talent.</p>
<p>Such a talented and extremely hardworking person had actually been imitated by someone in a short battle. Furthermore, the combat strength he displayed wasn’t inferior to Jiuyang’s. Shenluo found it unbelievable.</p>
<p>This Zhou Wen looks much more terrifying than expected. It’s no wonder Lord Holy God sent me to help Jiuyang. Indeed, Lord Holy God has foresight. I definitely can’t let such a fellow grow stronger. Otherwise, he will be a great enemy of my Holy Land. Killing intent flashed in Shenluo’s eyes..</p>
<h3 id='chapter1582'>Chapter 1582: Connate Appropriation</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>
<p>The Holy Land could tolerate a human with a powerful Companion Beast, but it couldn’t tolerate the existence of a person who was powerful enough to threaten the Holy Land.</p>
<p>Godsfall secretly rejoiced. Thankfully, Zhou Wen’s cultivation hasn’t reached an uncontrollable level. There’s still a chance of destroying him before he attains his full potential.</p>
<p>Godsfall was already secretly searching for a suitable opportunity to attack.</p>
<p>However, before killing Zhou Wen, Godsfall wanted to snatch his Companion Beast. From his point of view, there was no conflict between the two matters.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen’s main combat strength stemmed from his Companion Beast. As long as it was snatched from him, Zhou Wen would suffer a drop in strength. Killing him wouldn’t be difficult since it was useless having only a potent realm.</p>
<p>Godsfall no longer had the mood to watch the show. Instead, he stared intently at Zhou Wen, searching for the best opportunity to attack.</p>
<p>Now that Zhou Wen hadn’t summoned his Companion Beast and had suppressed his strength to the Epic stage, it could be said that this was the best opportunity for Godsfall. It was a god-sent opportunity.</p>
<p>Godsfall was the Connate Holy Temple’s Holy Son. The Essence Energy Art he cultivated was the same as Li Xuan’s Invincible Connate Divine Art.</p>
<p>However, Li Xuan cultivated an incomplete version, and not only did Godsfall cultivate the complete version, but it was also a modified version that had been supplemented by past Saints.</p>
<p>Unlike Jiuyang, Godsfall didn’t choose to contract a Guardian. Instead, he chose the path of Spirit Casting and devoured the Connate Ancient God Guardian.</p>
<p>Coupled with the Connate Holy Temple sparing no expense to groom him, Godsfall had reached the Hell level like Jiuyang thanks to the massive amount of resources.</p>
<p>Furthermore, the abilities that Godsfall was good at were different from the typical Connate Holy Temple Saint. His Life Providence, Life Soul, Wheel of Destiny, Terror transformation, and Calamity Zone were different from Li Xuan’s.</p>
<p>Li Xuan became stronger from being beaten up, but Godsfall could directly plunder the growth of others. It could be said that the two of them were at two extremities with some similarities.</p>
<p>The Calamity Zone of Godsfall was called “Connate Return” and was also called “Connate Appropriation.”</p>
<p>In his domain, he could appropriate the other party of everything other than their Connate body.</p>
<p>A Connate Body referred to one’s body of flesh and blood. Clothes, weapons, and accessories could be appropriated as long as they were external.</p>
<p>Companion Beasts were also foreign objects. Godsfall could also appropriate them.</p>
<p>However, Connate Appropriation wasn’t without restrictions. If Godsfall wanted to strip something, he had to come into contact with it. Furthermore, it needed to be used on living creatures.</p>
<p>Of course, the appropriation of a Companion Beast had to be done when Zhou Wen was alive. Once Zhou Wen died, the Companion Beast would transform into Essence Energy and dissipate back into the universe. Then there would be nothing to appropriate.</p>
<p>Under normal circumstances, as long as the enemy summoned a Companion Beast, Godsfall could snatch it for his own use.</p>
<p>However, Zhou Wen’s Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General was somewhat powerful. Godsfall didn’t wish for Zhou Wen to have a chance to resist, so he decided to attack Zhou Wen himself.</p>
<p>As long as he touched the Companion Beast tattoo—even if it was invisible—he could successfully appropriate it.</p>
<p>Therefore, what Godsfall needed to do was actually determine where the Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General was located on Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>This wasn’t difficult to determine. There was a general rule. For example, armor-type Companion Beasts were usually tattooed on one’s chest or back.</p>
<p>Weapon-type Companion Beasts were typically on one’s palms or arms.</p>
<p>Godsfall didn’t know what the Tiger Soul General’s companion form was, but from the looks of it, it was highly likely that it was similar to armor. Even if it wasn’t, such a Companion Beast was most likely on the chest or back. These were also the targets Godsfall chose.</p>
<p>As long as I snatch his Tiger Soul General, it will be easy for Jiuyang and me to kill him, Godsfall had already made up his mind. He was just waiting for an opportunity to succeed in one strike.</p>
<p>In order to increase his success rate, Godsfall planned on touching Zhou Wen’s body as much as possible. It wouldn’t be a problem to appropriate more Companion Beasts. Regardless, he couldn’t miss the Tiger Soul General. Otherwise, it would be troublesome once Zhou Wen summoned it.</p>
<p>Godsfall didn’t know that even if Zhou Wen were to summon the Tiger Soul General, it wouldn’t be as powerful as he had seen on the Cube.</p>
<p>There was no heat here at all. The Tiger Soul General had no way of accumulating the demonic flames in his body, nor did he have the time to temper his body. His level was only at the Human Realm, so he was basically no threat to Godsfall and Jiuyang.</p>
<p>Godsfall didn’t know this, so he was determined to obtain the Tiger Soul General. Godsfall even wanted to use the Tiger Soul General to kill Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen, oh Zhou Wen, blame it on yourself for becoming enemies with the Holy Land and and on your overestimation of your abilities. Godsfall took the opportunity to instantly appear behind Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>Godsfall was good at the Connate Breath technique. In the senses of others, Godsfall was no different from a rock on the ground. If one didn’t see him with their own eyes, it would be difficult to discover his existence.</p>
<p>Despite being extremely careful, Zhou Wen failed to discover him.</p>
<p>At the instant Godsfall approached, he clung his entire body to Zhou Wen’s back. His hands wrapped around him and pressed down on Zhou Wen’s chest.</p>
<p>The Connate Appropriation took effect. The clothes covering the area vanished just before Godsfall touched Zhou Wen’s body.</p>
<p>Bang!</p>
<p>Zhou Wen’s reaction was extremely fast. In an instant, the Chaos Egg had already burgeoned from his body and sent Godsfall flying.</p>
<p>Godsfall’s figure spun in midair and landed on the ground like a ghost. He licked his lips and stared smilingly at Zhou Wen with his slender eyes.</p>
<p>“Egg Sovereign! So Zhou Wen is Egg Sovereign!” Youkai shouted when he saw the Chaos Egg over Zhou Wen’s body.</p>
<p>Carlos was first slightly taken aback and then enlightened before he said, “I see. It’s no wonder Jiuyang challenged Zhou Wen to a duel. I should have known.”</p>
<p>In fact, it couldn’t be blamed on Carlos. It was mainly because the Tiger Soul General’s performance was too domineering, No one believed that Zhou Wen could obtain its Companion Egg from killing the corresponding dimensional creature. Previously, the main speculation by people was that Egg,</p>
<p>Sovereign was Human Sovereign. They didn’t think of Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>Their guess wasn’t wrong, but no one expected Human Sovereign to be Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>“Inever expected the Holy Land to think highly of me. They even laid an ambush with a Saint here to wait for me,” Zhou Wen said with a frown. He had already vaguely sensed that something was amiss with his Companion Beasts.</p>
<p>“Godsfall, why are you here?” Jiuyang also frowned and asked Godsfall.</p>
<p>“To help you complete the mission,” Godsfall said indifferently.</p>
<p>“This is my business. I don’t need you,” Jiuyang said coldly.</p>
<p>“This is an order from Lord Holy God.” With that said, Godsfall ignored Jiuyang and looked at Zhou Wen with a smile. “Zhou Wen, it’s our first time meeting. My name is Godsfall, a Saint from the Connate Holy Temple. Don’t forget my name in what’s left of your short life..”</p>
<h3 id='chapter1583'>Chapter 1583: Snatching Companion Beasts</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>
<p>“What did you do to me?” Zhou Wen asked as he checked his body.</p>
<p>He could clearly sense that there was something wrong with many of his Companion Beasts. There was a faint force that seemed to lock onto a portion of his Companion Beasts.</p>
<p>It was especially so for the Companion Beasts on his back. This feeling was extremely intense. A similar situation happened at his chest where Godsfall had touched.</p>
<p>Godsfall smiled at Zhou Wen and said, “What I did was to hold your life in my hand. Your life is now in my hands.”</p>
<p>“Ido want to know how I’ll die,” Zhou Wen said indifferently.</p>
<p>“You mostly rely on your Companion Beasts, right?” As Godsfall spoke, he snapped his fingers.</p>
<p>With a snap, a hidden tattoo on Zhou Wen’s body automatically surfaced and flew out. Even the Chaos Egg failed to stop the Companion Beast from leaving.</p>
<p>Soon, a Poison Bat-like Companion Beast flew to Godsfall’s side and circled him twice before flying onto his back and turning into a tattoo.</p>
<p>“How can this be?” Carlos and Youkai were alarmed. They had never heard of anyone capable of snatching a person’s Companion Beast.</p>
<p>‘There was a powerful contractual force binding Companion Beasts. Once they hatched, they couldn’t even be transferred. If they were forcefully transferred, one had to pay a huge price or even pay with their lives.</p>
<p>Godsfall had actually snatched a Companion Beast from him. If this ability were to spread, it would probably cause panic in the Federation.</p>
<p>“Is that all?” Zhou Wen remained unmoved.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen had already seen similar powers from Liu Yun. Furthermore, Liu Yun’s technique was better than Godsfall’s.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen had roughly guessed that Godsfall needed to touch his Companion Beast tattoo to steal it. As for Liu Yun’s Star Stealer, it had long reached the stage of stealing pets out of thin air.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen had always wanted to learn Star Stealer, but he had never had it drop. This left him vexed.</p>
<p>“Is that all?” Godsfall’s expression turned cold as he raised his palms and clapped.</p>
<p>With a clap, another Companion Beast tattoo appeared on Zhou Wen’s body. This time, it wasn’t just one, but ten. All of them flew towards Godsfall.</p>
<p>Godsfall originally wanted to strike fear in Zhou Wen. Ordinary people would be horrified to have ten Companion Beasts stripped from him.</p>
<p>However, Godsfall soon realized that the ten Companion Beasts he had appropriated from Zhou Wen were all low-level Companion Beasts like Poison Bats, Runic Heavy-Armored Warriors, Steel Cauldron Sprites, and so on. He didn’t even get a single Mythical stage, much less Tiger Soul General.</p>
<p>“Any more?” Zhou Wen asked Godsfall.</p>
<p>He had many low-level Companion Beasts on him. Ignoring the Musical Note Sprites, he needed a large number of Runic Heavy-Armored Warriors, Steel Cauldron Sprites, and other Companion Beasts for fusion. He would farm them every now and then, so he had a lot of them. Furthermore, these</p>
<p>Companion Beast tattoos were mainly on his chest and back.</p>
<p>Godsfall’s expression changed slightly. He never expected Zhou Wen to have so many low-level Companion Beasts.</p>
<p>Although there were no restrictions on the number of Companion Beast contracts, having too many Companion Beasts was useless in battle. A person’s control was limited. It was not bad for an ordinary person to control two or three Companion Beasts while fighting.</p>
<p>It would be impressive even for some experts who cultivated psyche techniques to simultaneously control more than ten Companion Beasts.</p>
<p>Unless it was an extremely intelligent Companion Beast, summoning a large number of Companion Beasts was similar to having a disorderly mob. They might even become a burden, much less be of help.</p>
<p>Therefore, most people would choose Companion Eggs that were useful to them or excellent Companion Eggs for incubation. Most of the Companion Eggs they didn’t need were sold.</p>
<p>It was especially so for a high-level powerhouse like Zhou Wen. He had no interest in Companion Eggs below the Mythical stage. Even if he picked them up, he would give them to his friends and juniors or exchange them for the materials he needed.</p>
<p>It was very rare to have low-level Companion Beasts like Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>If Zhou Wen didn’t need them for fusion, he wouldn’t have had so many low-level Companion Beasts on him.</p>
<p>“Let’s see how many low-level Companion Beasts you have,” Godsfall said coldly as he clapped his hands again.</p>
<p>Pa! Pa! Pa! Pa! Pa!</p>
<p>Godsfall could only appropriate ten Companion Beasts for each Connate Appropriation. He could only sense that Connate Appropriation had locked onto Zhou Wen’s body, but he didn’t know how many Companion Beasts there were.</p>
<p>This was because no matter how many Companion Beasts there were, the tattoos would overlap. Furthermore, different Companion Beasts could appear in the same spot. Zhou Wen’s back and chest were densely covered with overlapping tattoos.</p>
<p>Godsfall could only sense the Companion Beast tattoos, but he didn’t know how many Companion Beasts there were or what Companion Beast they were.</p>
<p>His clapping wasn’t done at random, Every time he used Connate Appropriation, he expended a large amount of Essence Energy. Even if Godsfall had tremendous amounts of Essence Energy, this series of clapping made his forehead drip with sweat.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen’s Companion Beasts flew out like scattering flowers. More than a hundred Companion Beasts flew towards Godsfall.</p>
<p>Youkai and Carlos were deeply shocked by this scene. To them, Godsfall’s Connate Appropriation was an invincible divine technique.</p>
<p>With such an ability, he was an existence that could do whatever he wanted among humans.</p>
<p>After all, most humans relied on their Companion Beasts to fight. Who wouldn’t be afraid of Godsfall’s ability?</p>
<p>“Twonder if he can snatch a Guardian. If he can do so, it will be too terrifying,” Youkai muttered to himself.</p>
<p>They were alarmed, but Godsfall was so depressed that he nearly blew a gasket.</p>
<p>Godsfall clearly saw the Companion Beasts before they flew over. Many of them were low-level Companion Beasts he had seen previously. Even if he had never seen them before, there were many that looked familiar. Clearly, they were commonly-seen, low-level Companion Beasts.</p>
<p>Godsfall wasn’t sure if there were any higher-level Companion Beasts, but there was definitely no Tiger Soul General.</p>
<p>“Continue.” Zhou Wen stood there without moving, nor did he have any intention of attacking Godsfall. He wanted to know how many Companion Beasts Godsfall’s ability could snatch from him—he wanted to know the limits of this ability.</p>
<p>As for whether his important Companion Beast would be snatched away, Zhou Wen wasn’t too worried.</p>
<p>He had too many Companion Beasts on him. It wasn’t easy for Godsfall to win the luck of the draw—Companion Beasts that Zhou Wen valued. Furthermore, there weren’t many Companion Beasts that Zhou Wen valued.</p>
<p>Prisoned Dragon was in that area, but the Limitless Demon Dragon King wasn’t. It was located slightly lower.</p>
<p>Tiger Soul General was also situated in that region, but Zhou Wen wasn’t worried about it at all. If Godsfall really snatched Tiger Soul General, Liu Yun’s experience back then would be what was awaiting him..</p>
<h3 id='chapter1584'>Chapter 1584: Holy Artifact</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>
<p>Godsfall gritted his teeth and raised his hands to clap again. He refused to believe that Zhou Wen had all these trash Companion Beasts.</p>
<p>Pa! Pa! Pa! Pa! Pa!</p>
<p>After a series of clapping, Godsfall was covered in sweat. His eyes were red, and the veins on his forehead protruded.</p>
<p>‘The Companion Beasts on Zhou Wen’s body flew up like scattering petals of flowers in bloom and headed for Godsfall.</p>
<p>Carlos and Youkai were already stunned, but Zhou Wen was about to burst out laughing.</p>
<p>Godsfall’s luck was clearly not good. Among the Companion Beasts he snatched, there wasn’t even a Mythical Companion Beast, much less Prisoned Dragon. They were all Epic and Legendary Companion Beasts.</p>
<p>In fact, it wasn’t Godsfall’s bad luck. It could only be said to be expected.</p>
<p>After all, the combined ratio of Mythical and Terror-grade Companion Beasts was at most one in ten thousand. It wasn’t easy to get them from drawing one to two hundred Companion Beasts.</p>
<p>Ignoring ten consecutive draws, there was no guarantee of a successful draw of a Mythical Companion Beast even with a hundred consecutive draws.</p>
<p>After the Companion Beasts landed on Godsfall, they belonged to him. Upon receiving the information from the Companion Beasts, Godsfall’s pupils dilated as blood seeped out of the comer of his mouth.</p>
<p>This fellow… How many trash Companion Beasts does he have on him… Godsfall already knew that none of the Companion Beasts he had snatched were at the Mythical stage.</p>
<p>Even Zhou Wen didn’t know the answer to this question. He had farmed a large number of Companion Beasts for the sake of fusion. Although many low-level Companion Beasts were useless to others, their Life Providences, Life Souls, and skills might be good materials for fusion. Zhou Wen naturally</p>
<p>wouldn’t skip out on them. He had been constantly gathering Companion Beasts that were trash in the eyes of others.</p>
<p>Just the Companion Beasts on his back numbered in the tens of thousands. It would be difficult for Godsfall to extract the Tiger Soul General from them.</p>
<p>This was under the circumstances that Godsfall had made a relatively good choice. He hadn’t chosen the location of the Musical Note Sprites. Otherwise, if he tried drawing Companion Beasts from the hundreds of thousands of Musical Note Sprites, it would make Godsfall suffer a greater breakdown.</p>
<p>No… [can’t let this continue… That bastard is nuts… Why does he have so many trash Companion Beasts on him for no reason. From that detestable expression he’s wearing, he must still have many trash Companion Beasts. Godsfall also knew that he was at his Essence Energy limits. If he were to.</p>
<p>continue appropriating, he would collapse without Zhou Wen needing to do a thing.</p>
<p>From the looks of it, can only use the Connate Holy Temple’s Holy Artifact. Godsfall took a deep breath and suppressed the trembling he experienced due to his excessive Essence Energy expenditure.</p>
<p>‘The six Holy Temples each had a Holy Artifact. Only Saints chosen by the Holy Temples had the right to possess it.</p>
<p>Four Holy Temples had finished choosing the wielders of the Holy Artifacts: the Trajectory Holy Temple’s Xiao, the Sun God Holy Temple’s Jiuyang, and the Connate Holy Temple’s Godsfall.</p>
<p>The so-called Holy Artifacts were actually special items born from the combination of the Holy Temple’s dimensional powers and Earth’s powers.</p>
<p>The dimension’s powers were originally suppressed by the rules on Earth, making it difficult for them to show their true effects.</p>
<p>However, because it combined the powers of Earth itself, this suppression didn’t exist. However, only one such Holy Artifact was born in every temple. As it took a long time to produce one, it was impossible for a second one to be produced unless another period as long as the time between the last</p>
<p>Mythical era to the present happened.</p>
<p>Furthermore, it wasn’t as simple as production. Although a Holy Artifact was produced, it was only in its embryonic form. Its abilities were very limited.</p>
<p>As Earth constantly and rapidly evolved in recent years, the Holy Temple had extracted more power from Earth allowing it to truly take form.</p>
<p>‘The Connate Holy Temple’s Holy Artifact was called “Connate Insight.” It was a stone talisman that looked like a comma. On one side of the stone talisman was a long horizontal carving, and on the other side was a short horizontal carving.</p>
<p>The power of the Connate Insight was very mysterious, as though it had the ability to predict the future. However, this ability needed external help to trigger it, but not by any external power.</p>
<p>Even among Saints who cultivated the Invincible Connate Divine Art, there weren’t many people who could activate the Connate Insight. Only Godsfall could truly use it.</p>
<p>Godsfall extended his palm and the ancient stone talisman floated above it. As his Essence Energy Art circulated, it surged into the stone talisman.</p>
<p>The two vertical marks on both sides of the stone talisman emitted a strange light. As for the stone talisman itself, it gradually spun. Soon, the speed at which it spun made it impossible to see its original appearance.</p>
<p>The stone talisman in Godsfall’s hand looked like a constantly spinning and changing Taiji sphere that emitted an infinite mysterious aura.</p>
<p>“Godsfall, put away your Holy Artifact. Zhou Wen is my target. I can finish him myself,” Jiuyang said with a frown.</p>
<p>“Don’t worry. I’ll leave him to you, but I want his Tiger Soul General.” Godsfall’s sleeves fluttered as the light from Connate Insight grew stronger. It made Godsfall’s face appear strange.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was originally alarmed as he wondered if he should retreat.</p>
<p>However, after hearing what Godsfall said, he felt relieved and dispelled the thought of retreating. He stared at the Holy Artifact in Godsfall’s hand that was changing like a Taiji sphere, wanting to know what use it had.</p>
<p>In the future, he would have to fight the Holy Land, so it was better to learn more about it now.</p>
<p>With the Chaos Egg protecting him, Zhou Wen didn’t panic.</p>
<p>As the power of the Connate Insight became stronger, Godsfall’s entire body seemed to be affected by it. The Connate aura circulated between the man and the talisman, causing Godsfall to undergo a complete transformation.</p>
<p>Godsfall was like an ancient god. His eyes seemed to have six illusory, intersecting lines. They were like lightning as he stared at Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen felt uncomfortable as though he was being peeped at with his clothes stripped off. In the next second, Godsfall suddenly shouted, “It’s him!”</p>
<p>As Godsfall shouted, he extended his right thumb and middle finger and snapped his fingers.</p>
<p>Pa!</p>
<p>Although he was still using Connate Appropriation, the snap of his fingers was like a bolt from the blue. There was even a bolt of lightning that lit up between his fingers, illuminating the entire Forbidden Land of the Gods.</p>
<p>After the thunderclap sounded, Zhou Wen felt his body relax as though a thousand tonnes of weight had been lifted off his body. A Companion Beast was forcefully separated from him, transforming into a mecha general that rode a ferocious tiger. It ran towards Godsfall in midair. It was none other than</p>
<p>the Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen watched in surprise as the Tiger Soul General flew towards Godsfall. He was alarmed. He actually managed to snatch the Tiger Soul General from me. That Holy Artifact is interesting!</p>
<p>‘The Tiger Soul General wasn’t a Companion Beast that could be easily snatched away. Zhou Wen couldn’t shake it off even if he wanted to, so it was even harder for others to snatch it.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen still remembered that the last time Eldest Senior Brother Liu Yun managed to snatch the Tiger Soul General was when he used the Zhang family’s ancestral Fate Reversal Talisman. Furthermore, the Tiger Soul General’s level was relatively low back then.</p>
<p>Now that the Tiger Soul General could still be snatched away despite being at the Calamity grade, this piqued Zhou Wen’s interest in the stone talisman.</p>
<h3 id='chapter1585'>Chapter 1585: Tiger Soul General Appropriated</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>
<p>‘When Godsfall saw Tiger Soul General fly towards him, he revealed a gratified smile and thought to himself, Although the process was a little tricky, I still completed the mission.</p>
<p>After Tiger Soul General landed on Godsfall, Godsfall looked down at Zhou Wen and said indifferently, “You should be proud to be able to force me to use the Holy Artifact.”</p>
<p>However, when Godsfall sensed the information from Tiger Soul General, he was stunned. He almost couldn’t believe the information he had received.</p>
<p>“Impossible. How can it only be at the Human Realm?” At that instant, Godsfall thought that he had snatched a fake Tiger Soul General.</p>
<p>From Tiger Soul General’s performance on Dubhe, he was undoubtedly at the Hell level. Furthermore, he had to be a top existence at the Hell level. Only then could he possess such might and easily kill two Starlord Ravenous Wolves.</p>
<p>Therefore, Godsfall found it unbelievable that Tiger Soul General was only at the Human Realm.</p>
<p>However, the Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General’s name wasn’t wrong and its appearance was right. It couldn’t be fake. After all, Calamity-grade Companion Beasts were relatively rare. Zhou Wen couldn’t have two identical Calamity-grade Companion Beasts, right? The chances were too low.</p>
<p>Could it be that Tiger Soul General is really that strong? He can kill Hell-level creatures at the Human Realm? Godsfall had his suspicions.</p>
<p>Apart from the difference in physical attributes, there was also the evolutionary difference of the Calamity Zone. A Hell-level domain would undergo a qualitative change.</p>
<p>For example, the two domains of fire and water that were both at the Human Realm might be able to mutually restrain each other, but if one domain advanced to the Hell level, it would completely crush the other.</p>
<p>Godsfall only noticed Tiger Soul General’s level and ability, but he didn’t have the time to carefully study his skills. Therefore, he didn’t realize how terrifying the Jinxes Master skill was.</p>
<p>“Zhou Wen, is this the Tiger Soul General you used to kill the Starlord Ravenous Wolves?” Godsfall summoned Tiger Soul General and asked Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>Although he felt that the possibility of Zhou Wen possessing two Tiger Soul Generals wasn’t high, Godsfall still wanted to get to the bottom of it.</p>
<p>“It’s whatever you make it to be.” Zhou Wen looked at Godsfall with a look of pity.</p>
<p>It was fine if he possessed Tiger Soul General, but to actually summon it—even Liu Yun hadn’t been as arrogant as him.</p>
<p>“I’s best you answer my question. Otherwise, even if you still have Tiger Soul General, only death awaits you. With the Holy Artifact, I already have the power of the Heaven level. I’m already an invincible existence in the human world.” Godsfall held the Connate Insight in his hand as his body emitted a</p>
<p>resplendent divine light that nearly illuminated the pitch-blacke Forbidden Land of the Gods.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen frowned as he looked at Godsfall. He could sense that Godsfall wasn’t bragging.</p>
<p>‘The strength of his aura had indeed exceeded the Hell-level creatures Zhou Wen had seen. It was highly likely that he had reached the Heaven level.</p>
<p>“What’s this so-called Holy Artifact? It actually has such a terrifying effect.” Zhou Wen had greater interest in the Connate Insight in Godsfall’s hand.</p>
<p>Although the Heaven level was very strong, Zhou Wen had the Chaos Egg, It shouldn’t be a problem for him to stay alive for the time being, so he didn’t have to be afraid.</p>
<p>“You think you have what it takes to deem yourself invincible in the human world?” As Zhou Wen spoke, he stared at Tiger Soul General.</p>
<p>He found it odd. Why wasn’t Godsfall suffering from bad luck? Liu Yun had suffered tremendously the moment he stole Tiger Soul General.</p>
<p>Could it be that Godsfall is like me and doesn’t fear Jinxes Master? Or could it be that Jinxes Master is useless after being augmented by that Holy Artifact? Zhou Wen thought to himself.</p>
<p>“Jiuyang, you heard it too. He’s the one who’s tempting fate. Don’t blame me for not leaving him to you.” As Godsfall spoke, the Connate aura on his body became even more terrifying. The Connate Insight entered a state of flux. Like a miracle, it emitted Connate Divine Light.</p>
<p>The entire Forbidden Land of the Gods was illuminated by divine light. The light over at Sunset City paled in comparison as though it was daytime everywhere.</p>
<p>Godsfall was about to walk towards Zhou Wen when he suddenly heard a strange sound, as though something had shattered.</p>
<p>Then, he saw specks of starlight appear in the Forbidden Land of the Gods.</p>
<p>The dilapidated city bricks, the cracked ground, the broken stone pillars, the barren desert, and the shattered ground were filled with specks of light.</p>
<p>Just like fireflies, they flew out from all directions and floated towards the sky. It was like a snowstorm that arose from underground. Countless snowflake-like points of light drilled out from the ground and flew up in the opposite direction. The scene was extremely strange, but it was also extremely</p>
<p>spectacular.</p>
<p>“What’s that?” Godsfall looked at the snowflake-like points of light and was somewhat puzzled.</p>
<p>It wasn’t just Godsfall. Everyone was alarmed and puzzled, unsure what the snowflakes that suddenly appeared were.</p>
<p>It’s coming… It’s coming… Zhou Wen was somewhat excited.</p>
<p>In fact, he didn’t know what the snowflake-like points of light were. However, he had a nagging feeling that the sudden appearance of these snowflakes was related to Tiger Soul General.</p>
<p>The points of light constantly condensed in the sky as they snowballed. Although no one knew what it was, the terrifying energy fluctuations in the snowball left everyone alarmed.</p>
<p>“Stop gaslightin;</p>
<p>” Godsfall held the Connate Insight in his hand and transformed into a Connate Divine Light that struck the huge snowball in the sky.</p>
<p>The Connate Divine Light was indomitable and could destroy virtually anything in the world. However, when it struck the snowball, it was like water being soaked up by a sponge as it seeped into the snowball.</p>
<p>The snowball that was originally emitting light became even brighter. As for the snowflakes that flew out of everything, they flew towards the snowball at an even faster speed and fused with it.</p>
<p>The points of light that seemed to be snow appeared to have accelerators activated as they charged towards the huge snowball in the sky.</p>
<p>Godsfall was first taken aback before he realized the problem.</p>
<p>These snowflake-like points of light weren’t caused by anyone. They seemed to have appeared because of his Connate power and the Connate Insight.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen naturally saw this scene. His thoughts were the same as Godsfall. The points of light were definitely affected by the Holy Artifact.</p>
<p>However, he went one level deeper than Godsfall. He felt that this coincidence might not be a pure coincidence. Perhaps it was thanks to Tiger Soul General.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen carefully sensed the energy fluctuations of the points of light, hoping to know what kind of power it was.</p>
<p>However, the energy fluctuations of the points of light were very special. He could only sense the existence of energy, but he couldn’t tell what attributes it had.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen extended his finger and touched a point of light with his fingertip. Immediately, he felt a strange force enter his body from his fingertip.</p>
<p>This power… Zhou Wen widened his eyes in disbelief..</p>
<h3 id='chapter1586'>Chapter 1586: Terrifying Jinxes Master</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>
<p>Zhou Wen became alarmed when he felt the power in the point of light.</p>
<p>This power was actually attracted by the Heaven-Opening Scripture of the Highest Elder. It flew towards the Heaven-Opening Scripture engraving on the Wheel of Destiny and landed in it, disappearing with a flash.</p>
<p>Could these things… be parts of the shattered Zone Core of the Forbidden Land of the Gods? Zhou Wen’s expression changed as he looked at the points of light.</p>
<p>More and more points of light flew towards the snowball in the sky at an accelerated pace. In just a moment, countless points of light gathered together, forming a huge cloud-like blob of light in the sky.</p>
<p>Godsfall used Connate Insight, but he failed to dissipate the light blob with one strike. Instead, he boosted the power of the light blob. He immediately knew that this thing was likely triggered by his strength.</p>
<p>After some thought, Godsfall gathered his strength and charged at Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>Regardless of what the blob of light was, all he needed to do was kill Zhou Wen and leave the Forbidden Land of the Gods before that thing fully formed.</p>
<p>He held the Connate Insight in one hand and grabbed at Zhou Wen with the other. Zhou Wen immediately felt an immense suction force suck the Chaos Egg towards his palm.</p>

<p>Light shone brightly in the sky as a beam of light suddenly shot down from the ball of light. Like lightning, it struck Godsfall’s head.</p>
<p>Godsfall was alarmed, but he couldn’t dodge the lightning, All he could do was gather his strength to resist it.</p>
<p>Lightning struck Godsfall’s head, but it didn’t produce any sparks or electric bolts. Godsfall’s body trembled as his legs went limp and he fell to the ground.</p>
<p>‘The Connate aura on his body instantly vanished without a trace, resulting in the Connate Insight losing its driving force and dimming. It stopped spinning and turned back into the stone talisman before falling to the ground.</p>
<p>As for the blob of light in the sky, it became even more dazzling as it smote down with lightning.</p>
<p>Godsfall’s expression changed drastically as he hurriedly gathered his strength again. However, he had none left. He wanted to dodge, but it was too late. All he could do was summon a bird-shaped Companion Beast to shield his head.</p>

<p>Youkai and Carlos turned around and ran. Who knew if the blob of light would treat them as its next target after killing Godsfall.</p>

<p>“Jiuyang… Save me…” The aging Godsfall was like an old man. It was difficult for him to even struggle to his feet. He used all his strength to cry to Jiuyang for help, but he only let out an extremely weak and hoarse voice.</p>
<p>‘When the third bolt of lightning struck down, Jiuyang’s body emitted light as he condensed the Sun God Light and smote the lightning that descended from the sky.</p>
<p>The lightning seemed bent on hitting Godsfall. Before it collided with the Sun God Light, it strangely vanished. When Jiuyang saw it again, the lightning had landed on Godsfall.</p>
<p>“Ah!” As the third bolt of lightning descended, Godsfall let out a tragic cry. The flesh on his body shriveled at a discernible pace.</p>
<p>A layer of withered skin clung tightly to the bones, almost no different from a skeleton.</p>
<p>However, Godsfall didn’t die just like that. His eyes protruded due to the shrinking of his flesh. They were filled with horror and despair.</p>
<p>With his current body, it was difficult for him to even crawl up. Alll that was left was death.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was alarmed when he saw this. After all, he was at the Hell level, and comparable to a Heaven-level powerhouse with the use of the Connate Insight. Yet, he still ended up in such a state.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen didn’t feel any pity for him, but when he thought of Godsfall’s outcome and how he might have been harmed by Jinxes Master, he felt uncomfortable.</p>
<p>Tiger Soul General had always followed him in the past. Furthermore, he had an even more ferocious Bamboo Blade resulting in double the Jinxes Master. He was lucky that nothing had happened to him.</p>
<p>In the past, he only felt that Jinxes Master had some influence like resulting in him getting hurt, but it wouldn’t lead to his death.</p>
<p>However, to see Godsfall reduced to such a state left Zhou Wen’s heart trembling as his legs went limp. It was a first.</p>
<p>Although it’s quite a pity, it can’t be considered a bad thing if Tiger Soul General dies with Godsfall, Zhou Wen thought.</p>
<p>He originally wondered if he should find an opportunity to retrieve Tiger Soul General, but after seeing Godsfall’s death, Zhou Wen felt that he should cherish his life and stay away from Jinxes Master.</p>
<p>After losing the Human Realm Tiger Soul General, he could still obtain other Companion Beasts. If for some reason he failed to hold back Jinxes Master one day, it wouldn’t be as simple as losing a Companion Beast. His life would be over.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was already considering whether he should throw the Bamboo Blade out. This was too terrifying, He didn’t wish to become like Godsfall.</p>
<p>Now wasn’t the time to think about this. Zhou Wen and Carlos reacted the same way. They turned around and prepared to run, Who knew if that thing would treat them as its next target after killing Godsfall?</p>
<p>Godsfall had Tiger Soul General, and he had the Bamboo Blade. They were both lethal things.</p>
<p>Just as Zhou Wen was about to run, he heard a boom. An explosion sounded from the blob of light as another bolt of lightning struck down.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen originally imagined that the lightning was aimed at Godsfall to kill him, but to his surprise, the lightning didn’t strike at Godsfall. Instead, it came at him.</p>
<p>Holy sh*t! Zhou Wen was so frightened that he immediately instant transmitted, hoping to dodge the lightning.</p>
<p>However, it was useless. The bolt of lightning struck him amidst his instant transmission, blasting him back into reality.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was blasted out in an instant. No matter how strong his previous opponent was, they could at most strike him down before he instant transmitted or after he completed it. He had never encountered such a situation.</p>
<p>Godsfall, who was on his last breath, seemed to feel a little more delighted when he saw Zhou Wen being struck by the lightning.</p>
<p>“Come to hell with me.” Godsfall gritted his teeth, his hoarse voice almost inaudible..</p>
<h3 id='chapter1587'>Chapter 1587: Condensing a Zone Again</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>
<p>Zhou Wen felt his heart palpitate. All he could do was pin his hopes on the Chaos Egg, hoping that it could withstand the power of the lightning.</p>

<p>Even the activated Heaven-Opening Scripture of the Highest Elder and Truth Listener were useless.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen shivered as the Chaos Egg automatically dissipated, exposing his body.</p>
<p>It’s over! Zhou Wen’s body and mind trembled as he felt his calves and stomach cramp. He was only human, one that was afraid of death. In particular, he didn’t want to end up like Godsfall.</p>
<p>He wanted to resist, but he realized that his Essence Energy was instantly sucked away by the lightning that invaded his body.</p>
<p>His Essence Energy was like iron powder, and the lightning was like a magnet. The former was instantly sucked dry, leaving nothing behind.</p>

<p>Upon seeing this scene, Godsfall laughed crazily. His face was as warped as a devil’s.</p>
<p>However, Godsfall’s smile quickly froze.</p>
<p>‘When he had been struck by the second lightning bolt, his body had rapidly aged and lost its vitality. However, none of that happened after Zhou Wen was struck by the second lightning bolt.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen’s aura didn’t weaken; it even became stronger. It was as though an intangible force was erupting from his body.</p>
<p>Jiuyang was slightly taken aback as he stopped and looked at Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>Rumble!</p>
<p>Explosive booms sounded from the light blob in the sky as the bolts of lightning formed a thunderstorm that constantly struck Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen seemed to be bathed in lightning, but his body didn’t wither like Godsfall. Instead, his aura became stronger and stronger.</p>
<p>“Impossible… Impossible…” Godsfall widened his eyes as though he had gone mad. He cried out angrily, but his voice was so hoarse that it was difficult to hear.</p>

<p>From the looks of it, that thing is indeed the Zone Core that was shattered back then. Furthermore, it happens to be compatible with my Heaven-Opening Scripture of the Highest Elder. It has benefited me. Instantly, Zhou Wen felt mixed emotions.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen didn’t know if this was considered luck. Although he had previously discovered that the Heaven-Opening Scripture of the Highest Elder could absorb the points of light, he wouldn’t have had the chance to absorb it if Godsfall hadn’t attracted the shattered Zone Core out.</p>
<p>I wonder what the Zone Core looked like before it was shattered? Zhou Wen stared at the blob of light in the sky and realized that it was gradually shrinking.</p>
<p>The blob of light was clearly not the true face of the Zone Core. It was only a collection of fragments. There was no Inowing what the real Zone Core looked like.</p>
<p>Unless one chanced upon an ancient powerhouse who had participated in the battle, it was very difficult to know what the core looked like.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen was actually somewhat puzzled. This Zone Core was already so terrifying in its shattered state. It could easily kill the Holy Artifact-wielding Godsfall; how powerful would it be when it was complete?</p>
<p>This Zone Core was clearly extraordinary to have so many powerhouses vie for it.</p>
<p>‘More and more words appeared on the Heaven-Opening Scripture of the Highest Elder. Finally, it began condensing a domain power. Zhou Wen could sense that the power of the Heaven-Opening Scripture was building a nomological domain.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen’s body floated in the air as a strange force spread out from his body.</p>
<p>These were the original ancient city ruins. Nearby, the ancient city ruins within the domain’s range were undergoing a strange change.</p>
<p>The broken walls, stone pillars, and ground were like a movie playing backwards as they were restored to their former appearance.</p>
<p>‘The weathered bricks were gradually repaired, and broken stone pillars appeared out of thin air. The entire ancient city seemed to be undergoing a reversal of time.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen… Is he condensing a domain to advance to the Calamity grade? Carlos couldn’t move his eyes away when he saw the strange magical scene.</p>
<p>After running for a short distance, they realized that something was amiss. When they turned their heads and saw this scene, they were stunned.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen… He seems to have a pure human body… Youkai sized up Zhou Wen’s body as his expression tured even odder.</p>
<p>It wasn’t just Youkai. Jiuyang also discovered the same problem. Zhou Wen didn’t have any traces of Spirit Casting on him, nor did he have the characteristics of a dimensional creature after using the Mythical Serum. No matter how he looked at it, he was a pure human.</p>
<p>He’s advancing to the Calamity grade as a pure human? Jiuyang stood there and looked at Zhou Wen in a daze..</p>
<h3 id='chapter1588'>Chapter 1588: Regicide</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>
<p>Jiuyang had always believed that Zhou Wen had used some method to advance to the Calamity grade. Now, he suddenly realized that Zhou Wen was condensing a domain. Furthermore, it was completely different from what he had imagined. Zhou Wen seemed to be a pure-blooded human without using</p>
<p>any external help.</p>
<p>Can pure-blooded humans really reach this stage? Jiuyang looked at Zhou Wen with a complicated expression.</p>
<p>Godsfall’s expression was even more complicated. He didn’t have any blood left to vomit. Otherwise, he would’ve definitely vomited another three liters of blood.</p>
<p>He had lost his vitality from being struck by the lightning. Zhou Wen had been struck by the same lightning, but he ended up advancing to the Calamity grade. There was no justice in this world.</p>
<p>It shouldn’t be like this… It shouldn’t be like this… The resentment in Godsfall’s heart couldn’t be appeased. He used his last breath to order the Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General to kill Zhou Wen. Even if he couldn’t kill Zhou Wen, it was fine if he could interrupt his advancement to the Calamity grade.</p>
<p>The Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General accepted the order and turned to look at Zhou Wen. The purple flames in his eyes constantly flickered, but he didn’t immediately rush over.</p>

<p>the Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General walk back?</p>

Be it his Life Providence, Life Soul, Wheel of Destiny, Terror transformation, Calamity Zone, or</p>

<p>Godsfall’s head fell to the ground as his eyes nearly popped out. It was obvious how he couldn’t accept his death.</p>
<p>The Companion Beast tattoo on his body dissipated with his death, turning into Essence Energy that returned to the universe.</p>
<p>However, the Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General remained standing proudly on his mount without any signs of dissipating.</p>
<p>This strange scene made everyone shudder. If Companion Beasts could kill their masters, then with so many Companion Beasts on them, they wouldn’t even know how they died if a Companion Beast attacked them one day. There was no way to defend against it.</p>
<p>The blob of light in the sky shrank as the domain power emitted from Zhou Wen’s body intensified. The restoration of the ancient city nearby sped up.</p>
<p>Ancient buildings were erected out of thin air, gradually restoring the ancient city to its original appearance.</p>
<p>Strange. Could it be that the Heaven-Opening Scripture’s domain is a Time Reversal Zone? Zhou Wen was somewhat puzzled.</p>
<p>The power displayed by the domain now was like reversing time, but the Heaven-Opening Scripture of the Highest Elder had nothing to do with temporal powers. From the beginning to now, he had never used a temporal item to advance.</p>
<p>No, it’s not temporal, Zhou Wen quickly realized the problem.</p>
<p>If it was a reversal of time, not only would the ancient city be restored, but everything inside would also be restored.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen didn’t know if there were any residents in the ancient city in the past, but there would definitely be creatures destroying it. If time flowed back, the creatures that destroyed the ancient city should have appeared in the reverse flow of time.</p>
<p>Now, only the ancient city was being restored. The creatures that had destroyed it didn’t appear. Furthermore, upon careful inspection, one would discover that many places in the domain hadn’t changed because of the domain’s power. Only the ancient city had changed.</p>
<p>‘What kind of domain is this? Zhou Wen kept sensing the domain’s power, but he still couldn’t understand what kind of domain it was.</p>
<p>The power of a domain was formed from two parts. One was the Essence Energy Art that one cultivated, including the Life Providence, Life Soul, Wheel of Destiny, and Terror transformation formed during the cultivation of the Essence Energy Art. These would have a certain effect on the domain’s</p>
<p>abilities.</p>
<p>The other important component was the Zone Core that one absorbed.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen could sense the portion of the Essence Energy Art, but he didn’t know what kind of power the Zone Core gave him. He also needed to constantly discover the domain’s abilities.</p>
<p>From the beginning, when the Zone Core severely injured Godsfall, its power showed some form of devouring and absorption. However, now that Zhou Wen had absorbed the Zone Core’s power, it produced an effect similar to the reverse flow of time. This made Zhou Wen momentarily unable to</p>
<p>determine what kind of ability the domain condensed by the Dao Sutra was.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen also thought of another possibility. If one’s Essence Energy Art and Zone Core combined to produce a domain, producing a special reaction, it might also trigger a domain ability that was different from both.</p>
<p>Just like a chemical reaction, the combination of two different elements could form a new material.</p>
<p>Of course, this was only Zhou Wen’s guess. Perhaps it wasn’t a new ability. It was only because Zhou Wen didn’t know much about the Zone Core’s abilities.</p>
<p>Boom!</p>
<p>Only a tiny portion of the blob of light remained. This portion transformed into a huge pillar of light that blasted at Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>As the pillar of light descended on Zhou Wen, the entire Forbidden Land of the Gods began to tremble. It was as though a huge earthquake had happened. Cracks that spanned hundreds of kilometers appeared on the ground as everything collapsed.</p>
<p>The buildings in Sunset City collapsed one after another, and huge rifts opened beneath the city. Half of the city had already fallen, and the remaining parts were constantly sliding down.</p>
<p>The darkness in the sky seemed to be cut open like a curtain. It peeled off piece by piece, revealing the originally blue sky. The entire Forbidden Land of the Gods was collapsing.</p>
<p>So to advance to the Calamity grade, one needs to use the power of a dimensional zone as the price. Carlos seemed to understand something…</p>
<h3 id='chapter1589'>Chapter 1589: Zone Formation</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>
<p>Youkai was rejoicing, “Thankfully, you forced the evacuation of everyone in Sunset City. Otherwise, not many in Sunset City would have survived such a huge disaster.”7</p>
<p>‘The Forbidden Land of the Gods collapsed more and more violently. Carlos and Youkai didn’t dare stay any longer. They turned around and rushed towards the exit of the Forbidden Land of the Gods.</p>
<p>Thankfully, Carlos’s Guardian was already at the Terror grade. Otherwise, it was unknown if he could escape alive.</p>
<p>‘The entire Forbidden Land of the Gods collapsed except the area near Zhou Wen. The ancient city had mostly been restored.</p>
<p>The ancient city had a mysterious and ancient aura. Buildings made of rocks had a very simple design. There were basically no decorations. Occasionally, one could see extremely simple drawings on some walls. They were also abstract things like landscapes.</p>
<p>Is this ancient city built by humans or is it an ancient city that originally existed in the dimensional zone? Zhou Wen guessed.</p>
<p>However, just as he was sizing up the ancient city, it suddenly shattered and turned to dust that rose into the sky. When the ashes flew into the air, they vanished.</p>
<p>‘When the ancient city completely vanished, the Heaven-Opening Scripture of the Highest Elder finally completed its evolution and reached the Calamity grade. Its domain power had completely taken form.</p>
<p>It has finally advanced to the Calamity grade. Zhou Wen heaved a sigh of relief. This was a pleasant surprise.</p>
<p>He originally thought that he had made a wasted trip, but to his surprise, he raised the Dao Sutra to the Calamity grade and condensed a Calamity Zone.</p>
<p>However, up to now, Zhou Wen still didn’t know much about the Calamity Zones ability. He needed more time to understand it before he could figure out what kind of domain it was.</p>
<p>‘The dark Forbidden Land of the Gods no longer existed. The sky was blue. When the sunlight shone down, there were crisscrossed abysses everywhere.</p>
<p>Just as Zhou Wen was rejoicing, he saw a blob of purple light run towards him. Looking up, it was the Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General.</p>
<p>What’s going on? Shouldn’t he perish with Godsfall? Zhou Wen had been paying attention to the Heaven-Opening Scripture of the Highest Elder and the newly formed domain. He hadn’t paid attention to the situation outside the domain and didn’t see what had happened.</p>
<p>Upon seeing Godsfall’s corpse on the ground while the Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General was rushing towards him, he was somewhat surprised. Just as he was about to stop the Tiger Soul General’s charge, he saw the ferocious tiger leap up. The Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General transformed into a purple</p>
<p>flame that flew towards Zhou Wen’s body.</p>
<p>It was useless for Zhou Wen to block it. The Fiend-Armored Tiger Soul General transformed back into a tattoo and imprinted it on Zhou Wen’s body—back in its original spot.3</p>
<p>Holy sh*t.. This. What’s going on.. A Companion Beast can return on its own without dying with its master… Zhou Wen was truly alarmed. He looked at the headless corpse that was sliding down the valley and couldn’t help but cry out, ‘Was Godsfall’s head chopped off by Tiger Soul General?”</p>
<p>“He was the one who chopped it off,” Jiuyang said as he stood not far from Zhou Wen.</p>

<h3 id='chapter1593'>Chapter 1593: Bottom of the River</h3>
<h5>Translator: CKtalon</h5>

<p>Zhou Wen was alarmed as he hurriedly gathered his strength to escape the metal column’s suction force. However, he failed to withstand it. Even though he used all his strength, his body still slid towards the metal column.</p>
<p>The baby bear was even worse than Zhou Wen. Its claws scratched the ground, tearing through the rocks, but it still slid towards the metal column at an even faster rate than Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>With a thought from Zhou Wen, thousands of Sword Pills appeared out of thin air, transforming into swords that charged at the metal column.</p>
<p>Clang! Clang! Clang! Clang!</p>
<p>The Sword Pills struck the metal column, creating deep dents. If there was enough time, the metal column would probably be shattered by the Sword Pills.</p>
<p>However, the suction force on the metal column didn’t disappear. Zhou Wen and the baby bear were still sucked towards the dented metal column. Furthermore, the suction force was still increasing in intensity, pulling them towards it at faster speeds.</p>
<p>Come out! Zhou Wen summoned the Golden Wyrm Scissors and the Soul Mirror.</p>
<p>The Golden Wyrm Scissors transformed into a golden beam of light that snipped at the metal column. The Soul Mirror also used the Soul-IIluminating Divine Light on the metal column in a bid to store it inside.</p>
<p>Clang!</p>
<p>Just as the Golden Wyrm Scissors approached the metal column, it stuck to it like a piece of metal sucked by a powerful magnet.</p>
<p>The Soul Mirror’s Soul-IIluminating Divine Light shone on the metal column, but it didn’t react at all. It didn’t get stored in the Soul Mirror. Instead, the Soul Mirror was also sucked onto the metal column.</p>
<p>It’s too late! Zhou Wen gritted his teeth and used Teacher Domain.</p>
<p>In the domains that Zhou Wen had already condensed, Human Sovereign Sacrifices to the Heavens was a healing-type, while the Chaos Egg was a defensive-type. Only the usage of Teacher Domain remained unknown, so he decided to give it a try.</p>
<p>When the Teacher Domain was activated, an invisible domain immediately enveloped the river. Zhou Wen felt his body lighten as the suction force from the metal column vanished. The Golden Wyrm Scissors and Soul Mirror were also unsummoned by Zhou Wen.</p>
<p>The baby bear in the Teacher Domain stopped at the same time and was no longer pulled towards the metal column.</p>
<p>Although I still don’t know what abilities the Teacher Domain has, it looks rather useful. Zhou Wen stood in midair as Sword Pills appeared from the void.</p>
<p>A portion of the Sword Pills appeared beneath the baby bear and lifted it up. More Sword Pills charged at the metal column like a surging river, constantly striking it.</p>
<p>Clang! Clang! Clang! Clang!</p>
<p>The metal column constantly caved in and deformed from the impact. Shattered pieces of metal fell and landed in the river.</p>
<p>Crack!</p>
<p>The metal column above the water surface shattered and collapsed into the river, the result of Sword Pill’s bombardment.</p>
<p>However, the metal column above the river’s surface was only a very short portion. Such a strike didn’t seem to shake the foundation of the metal column.</p>
<p>With a thought from Zhou Wen, the Sword Pills charged into the river and constantly struck the metal column, shattering it inch by inch. Even the river water failed to lessen the Sword Pills’ attacks.</p>
<p>I want to see what’s up. Zhou Wen charged into the river with the infinite Sword Pills.</p>
<p>‘Wherever Zhou Wen stood, Sword Pills appeared out of thin air, warding off the river water. The Sword Pills constantly struck the metal column, shattering it.</p>
<p>However, the metal column was just too long. The parts Zhou Wen could sense exceeded a thousand meters. He didn’t know when he could completely destroy it if he continued bombarding it.</p>
<p>Therefore, after trying for a while, Zhou Wen gave up on the idea of completely destroying the metal column. He circled around it and, under the protection of the sword domain, headed deep into the river.</p>
<p>In the Calamity-grade sword domain, the Sword Pill particles were indestructible. Even if they dissipated, they only went from light to darkness. With a thought, Zhou Wen could switch them without expending any energy.</p>
<p>Zhou Wen dived a thousand meters, but he still failed to see the bottom of the river. Beneath him was still a bottomless river. The metal column seemed to have no end as it continued extending towards the bottom of the dark river.</p>
<p>“L don’t believe you have no end.” Zhou Wen continued charging down.</p>
<p>The lower he went, the stronger the suction force of the river. The suction force on the metal column became stronger.</p>
<p>However, with the protection of the Teacher Domain, the suction force was useless against Zhou Wen. The sword domain tore through the river and served as an aegis for Zhou Wen and the baby bear to rush into the depths of the river.</p>
<p>After diving for more than three thousand meters, Zhou Wen finally sensed the existence of the river’s bottom. At the same time, he saw the end of the metal column.</p>
<p>Beneath the metal column was a gigantic toad. It was jade-white and crystalline, and it suffused a holy halo.</p>
<p>The combination of ugliness and holiness looked extremely strange.</p>
<p>‘The toad was constantly respiring in a bid to escape the suppression of the black metal column. The bubbles came from its mouth.</p>
<p>The black metal column pressed down on it. Every time it struggled, the black metal column would crush a parotoid gland on its body. Black-red liquid flowed out from it, dyeing the nearby river red.</p>
<p>As the toad exhaled, it produced a terrifying suction force that sucked everything nearby into its mouth.</p>
<p>Its mouth was like a bottomless pit that couldn’t be filled. And its main target was Zhou Wen..</p>
